After the Executive Yuan meeting on the 18th concluded its agenda, many members wished to understand the details of the Wanpaoshan and anti-Chinese Korean incidents. Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang was invited to the Executive Yuan to explain the details of these two incidents in detail. Since the meeting was not public and no journalists were present, the news reports are mostly conjecture and do not reflect the actual facts. Please correct this. Numbered by the Secretariat of the Legislative Yuan.

Special Article

The Red Peril and China's Survival (Continued)

Yang Xingfo

The Communists' distribution of land and resistance to rent are merely temporary means to lure peasants. Therefore, it is called a preliminary policy of in-depth land revolution. At the same time, fearing that the peasants would realize that the land they were dividing was merely a fleeting mirage, they vigorously prohibited party members from proposing the slogan "Confiscate all land," advocating for a communal farming system (i.e., a state-owned farm to realize the communist system) and using government laws or party resolutions to prohibit the sale and lease of land. The reason given is that these measures would alienate the Communist Party from the broad masses of peasants nationwide (see the current work plan for Soviet areas). However, the ultimate goal of the Communist Party's land program remains the elimination of landlords and the private land system and the realization of state ownership of land. The peasants who divide the land are merely straw dogs in the process of the party's land revolution. As for the Communist Party members retaining fertile land for themselves when distributing land or favoring relatives and friends, and still levying extremely heavy land taxes, these are obvious abuses that are not worth discussing.

The Communist Party's policy on popular organizations is to use the benefits of the land revolution to attract the basic masses in the countryside, the poor peasants, farm laborers, and coolies, to be the main force for their armed uprisings and class struggle. They temporarily maintain contact with middle peasants and completely oppose wealthy peasants, striving to exclude the wealthy peasant component from the government and all armed organizations. The benefits used to attract poor peasants, tenant farmers, and coolies are, in fact, taken from the wealthy peasants. If wealthy peasants also have political power and participate in armed organizations, then class struggle will inevitably lead to internal strife, and the distribution of benefits will be impossible. Popular organizations in the bandit areas, in both rural villages and cities, include handicraft workers' unions and coolies' unions. In addition, there are industrial workers' unions and shop employees' unions specifically in towns, and farm laborers' unions, poor peasant associations, and poor people's associations specifically in rural areas. Among them, farm laborers' unions are the most important. The Communist Party recognizes them as one of the important tools for realizing the leadership of the proletariat in the current democratic revolution. Each union is organized based on industry or occupation, with the district as the unit, and then there are village branches, general unions, and even the general union of the entire special zone. The general union prefixed with the name of a county or special city is composed of the general unions of various industries in urban and rural areas. The Communist Party also fully utilizes bandits and vagrants. The method is "to attract bandits and vagrant masses to obtain the benefits of the land revolution. The best way is to dissolve their inherent organizations, distribute land to them, and resolve their reactionary leaders, that is, to sympathize with revolutionary leaders, and at least not let him lead the original troops" (see the current work plan for the Soviet area). The secret societies of the Hongjiang Society and the Three Dots Society are all welcomed by them. The so-called slogan of welcoming Hongjia brothers refers to this. Although the Hong Gang forces in Jiangxi have declined recently, they provide red bandits with reconnaissance and information, which causes some disadvantage to the government troops. In addition, the Communist Party also absorbs old-style peasant armed organizations, such as the Small Swords Society and the Red Spears Society, as much as possible. Their method of dealing with them is similar to that of dealing with secret societies and bandits.

The Process of Suppressing the Reds – The Red Peril in China is most severe in the three provinces of Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan. Among the three provinces, Jiangxi is the most severe. The military strength of the Red bandits is almost entirely concentrated in Jiangxi. When Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping fled from Nanchang to Yiyang in the 16th year of the Republic (1927) during the Kuomintang's anti-communist campaign, they only carried seven guns. Now, the 10th Army of the Red Army under Fang Zhimin has more than 10,000 men and more than 2,000 guns. When Zhu De fled from Jiangxi to Hunan in the 16th year of the Republic (1927) and joined Mao Zedong, the number of guns was only two or three hundred. Now, the troops under Zhu De have more than 30,000 men and more than 10,000 guns. The speed at which the Red bandit forces have expanded can be seen from this. Three years ago, a small rabble of men now requires the mobilization of the country's troops, and Generalissimo Chiang himself has to go to the front lines before there is hope of extermination. Could this be what the sellers of local interests at the time dreamed of? Jiangxi has been afflicted by the Red Peril for nearly four years, and the active suppression of the Reds only began after the campaign against Yan and Feng. The influence of the civil war on the suppression of the Reds can be seen from this again.

The suppression of the Reds in Jiangxi can be divided into three periods: the first period was the period of suppression by Lu Diping; the second period was the period of suppression by He Yingqin; and the third period was the period of suppression by Chiang Kai-shek. In the 18th year of the Republic (1929), when Lu Diping was in charge of Jiangxi, he originally had troops from the 18th, 50th, 12th, and 3rd Divisions. Using these troops to suppress the Reds should have been able to cope. Subsequently, due to the re-emergence of the civil war, the 50th and 12th Divisions were transferred out of the province, leaving only the 18th and 13th Divisions to guard Jiangxi. The Red flames then spread daily, and more than 60 counties in Jiangxi were ravaged. The provinces of Hunan and Hubei all had troops stationed with the responsibility of suppressing the Reds, but each guarded its own boundaries and refused to cross the Lei River a step, so the bandits were able to move freely in the three provinces. Since the end of the military campaign against Yan and Feng last autumn, the Red Peril had become a prairie fire. The government then ordered the 50th and 12th Divisions to return to Jiangxi and transferred elite troops of about 17 divisions, totaling more than 100,000 men, to be under the command of Lu Diping. Although this campaign recovered the counties of Ji'an, the 18th Division was surrounded and annihilated in the bandit area, and the division commander, Zhang Huijiong, was captured and killed. The 50th Division was also badly defeated, losing more than half of its troops. The bandit forces revived. Although the reasons for the failure of this campaign are very complex, they can be seen from the six points mentioned by Brigade Commander Dai Yue: (1) The troops are frequently transferred, so that the remnant bandits who are about to be exterminated can revive; (2) The bandit suppression troops do not understand the situation and organization in the bandit areas; (3) The bandit suppression troops harbor sectarian views, intending to perfunctorily and not earnestly and thoroughly handle the suppression; (4) The county magistrates are incompetent and corrupt, the police discipline is poor, harassing the people everywhere, and the local bullies exploit and oppress the people, causing the people to suffer injustice and resentment, and to take risks; (5) The party, government, army, and people cannot cooperate effectively and consistently to eliminate the Communist bandits; (6) The rural economy is bankrupt, handicraft workers are unemployed, and the people's livelihoods are difficult. Coupled with the Communist bandits' enticements and threats, the number of poor people who follow them is increasing daily (see Dai's "A Little Contribution to Bandit Suppression and Village Cleansing").

After the failure of the first phase of bandit suppression, the government knew that the bandit forces were rampant and could not be ignored. It also realized that the failure of this campaign was due to the lack of unified command, so it sent Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin to act as Commander-in-Chief and to oversee the suppression in Jiangxi. After arriving in Jiangxi in February of this year, He took the strategy of Zeng Guofan, "steady progress and gradual advancement," based on the miscalculation of underestimating the enemy and going deep in the past. At the same time, he also had considerable plans for reorganizing the local areas, gathering refugees, and establishing county defense groups. There was also considerable progress in the military sphere. In May, the two Guangdong provinces became independent, and the bandit forces revived. Sun Lianzhong, Gong Bingfan, and Wang Jinyu's troops were successively defeated, and Hu Zuyu was killed while supervising the battle. At this point, the Central Government knew that it would be difficult to achieve the effect of suppression without using all its strength to suppress the Reds. People from all walks of life began to pay attention to the Red Peril in Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan. Generalissimo Chiang resolutely came to Jiangxi to oversee the suppression, and the elite of the country's troops gathered in Jiangxi. The third phase of the bandit suppression work began in July. At present, the number of troops and guns in the National Army in Jiangxi is more than 300,000. According to recent reports, Chen Mingshu on the right wing attacked Donggu, Sun Lianzhong in the center attacked Ningdu, and He Yingqin on the left wing attacked Guangchang, all making steady progress. The bandit suppression in this phase should be able to achieve the final victory according to the planned plan. However, the fundamental elimination of the Red bandits may not be realized in the short term, and it cannot rely solely on the military force of the army.

Discussion - The Red Peril today is not only a catastrophe since the establishment of the Republic of China, but also an unprecedented change in China for thousands of years. Social evolution changes when it reaches its end. Feudal system and patriarchal society China will disappear with the emperors and warlords. Will it be replaced by an independent and free China of the Three Principles of the People, or a Communist China that is a dependency of Soviet Russia? This is what all the people of the country, regardless of gender or age, should ask themselves. The military victory of suppressing the Reds is only a temporary solution. There are myriad aspects to military post-war management. If the people's livelihoods cannot be resolved and local politics cannot be improved, even without the Red bandits, how can the country last long? Moreover, local tyrants, corruption, and poverty are the breeding grounds for the Red Peril. Therefore, to fundamentally eliminate the Red bandits, the only way is to implement the Three Principles of the People. To implement the Three Principles of the People, there must be a long period of domestic peace. Today's political views inside and outside the party, no matter how different, are all details compared to the issue of national survival. We should strive to communicate and avoid civil war in order to promote the great unity of the country and jointly face the national crisis. Otherwise, it will either be Outer Mongolia under the aegis of Soviet Russia, or Korea under the trampling of the violent Japanese. I hope that my countrymen will not dismiss my words as irrelevant. (The End)

News Highlights

Central and National Government Memorial Week

▲ Cai Yuanpei Reports on the Wanxian Case and the Japanese

▲ Yu Youren Reports on the Suppression of Communist Bandits

▲ Central Party Headquarters: July 20th, 9:00 AM. The Central Party Headquarters held its 120th Memorial Week meeting in the Grand Auditorium. Attendees included Central Committee members Cai Yuanpei, Ding Weifen, Fang Juehui, Chen Lifu, Miao Peicheng, Yu Jingtang, and others, as well as staff from various departments and guests, totaling over 500 people. Ding Weifen chaired the meeting. After the salutations, Cai Yuanpei reported that the Wanbaoshan Incident originated from Koreans forcibly occupying farmland belonging to Chinese farmers and digging canals to divert water. Rioters in several places in Korea, including Pyongyang, Seoul, Incheon, Jinampo, Busan, Kaiyuan, Wonsan, and Sinuiju, indiscriminately slaughtered overseas Chinese. While some believe this was solely due to the agitation from the Wanbaoshan Incident, limiting it to a conflict between China and Korea, the underlying situation is more complex. On June 1st, the Changchun County government sent officials to persuade the Koreans to leave, but they refused. The officials then took eight of their leaders to the county office, where they confessed to being ordered by the Japanese to cultivate rice. On the 3rd, the Koreans involved in the expulsion process were driven out, but on the 4th, 100 Koreans were still working in the area, protected by five Japanese police officers. This shows that the land rental and canal digging were initiated entirely by the Japanese. After the Chinese farmers spontaneously filled the moats and destroyed the dikes, the Japanese police opened fire with live ammunition and increased their military police presence to over 500, which is even more evident. As for the atrocities in various places in Korea, they were incited by Japanese newspapers beforehand and condoned by police officials during the event. On the 4th, Japanese newspapers in Incheon, Korea, suddenly reported that Korean farmers in Wanbaoshan were massacred by Chinese farmers and that the Northeast authorities had ordered the expulsion of Korean residents. Koreans were greatly alarmed. That evening, Koreans held a city meeting to discuss the issue of Korean residents being persecuted. The Japanese authorities usually strictly prohibit Koreans from holding meetings, especially mass gatherings, but this time it was specially permitted. Uninformed Koreans became greatly indignant and marched in groups to the Chinese district to protest. Japanese police stood by and did nothing to stop them. The crowd threw stones near the Incheon Chinese Chamber of Commerce, damaging shops and initiating a conflict with the Chinese. Koreans then launched a large-scale attack on various Chinese shops. Some Korean intellectual groups distributed leaflets urging the crowd not to riot, but the Japanese police prevented them from doing so. The Japan Chronicle, a Japanese newspaper published in Kobe by a British man named Young, commented in its editorial on the 9th that the Pyongyang riot was the most violent, with dozens of Chinese people brutally beaten to death on the streets. The Japanese side cunningly claimed that the Japanese police were unable to stop it, in an attempt to shirk responsibility. During the brewing of the riot on the 3rd, rumors spread rampant in various places in Korea. What is most noteworthy is that Japanese people living among the overseas Chinese in Pyongyang had already moved elsewhere beforehand. On Saturday and Sunday, anti-Chinese riots broke out in Pyongyang, Seoul, Jemulpo, and Wonsan. That morning, the Chinese Consul-General in Korea personally went to the Governor-General's office, requesting protection for the overseas Chinese and warning the Japanese authorities of the spreading riots. The Seoul Chinese Chamber of Commerce also issued the same warning. Japanese officials all remained indifferent. Furthermore, the Tokyo Hochi Shimbun reported that the violent Pyongyang attack on Chinese people was premeditated. The ringleaders, who used a gathering on the 5th (Sunday) to discuss and direct the rioters inside a Christian church, all carried annotated maps indicating the locations of Chinese families. Police squads followed behind them. The ringleaders instructed the rioters with three rules: advance fiercely when encountering police officers, be cautious when encountering military police, and retreat when encountering the military. They also issued strict orders not to lay a finger on the Japanese. Therefore, in Pyongyang, where anti-Japanese sentiment was supposedly at its highest and unity was paramount, not a single Japanese person was harmed. Based on the above, it is sufficient to prove that the Japanese not only condoned this riot, but actually instigated and directed it. On the 6th, a Reuters dispatch stated that political circles in Tokyo were deeply distressed by the anti-Chinese military actions in Korea and feared that they would lead to a major disaster. This is because over 500,000 Koreans are scattered throughout Manchuria and Mongolia, and if the Chinese are provoked and take retaliatory action, the Chinese authorities will find it difficult to protect them, and the Japanese side will be unable to provide cover, which may lead to a major incident. These major incidents are what the Japanese hope for, as they will use the excuse of the Chinese authorities' inability to protect them to dispatch troops to protect their overseas residents, in order to fulfill their desire to invade Manchuria and Mongolia. Unexpectedly, the Chinese people are no longer as foolish as they were during the Boxer Rebellion. They all understand the meaning of having a cause for their grievances and a target for their debts, and have developed the habit of being gentle when appropriate and unyielding when necessary. They have always recognized the Koreans as victims and do not hate them. As for the Japanese, they feel that there are a few who understand things a little better, and do not regard all of them as enemies. All the Japanese people's schemes of self-inflicted injury have not worked. This recent goal of the Japanese people naturally stems from a consistent plan. Their plan is to implement a kind of immigration policy in Manchuria and Mongolia. When Goto, President of the South Manchuria Railway Company, was in office, he had a plan to immigrate three million people to Manchuria and Mongolia within twenty years, and said that if the immigration policy succeeds, the three eastern provinces will de facto become Japanese territory. The Japanese once made a chart and hung it everywhere: "Japan has 43,700 square miles and 85 million people; Manchuria has 65,000 square miles and 28 million people." Later, because the experiment of relocating Japanese residents failed, they changed their plan and moved Koreans to the three eastern provinces and Japanese to Korea. Japan wants to relocate Koreans, first by tricking them out of their property, making them homeless. The police station, based on household registration surveys, registers unemployed people one by one and finds ways to help them. When a certain period of time comes and a considerable number is reached, they announce the immigration plan, send them to Manchuria and Mongolia to cultivate land, and force them to register with the Japanese consulate, prohibit them from paying taxes to the Chinese authorities, and encourage them to resist the Chinese authorities. If Koreans suffer any losses due to conflicts between China and Korea, they immediately make demands for compensation, hoping to create a tense situation that may lead to actual war. Now the diplomatic organs have already made representations according to law regarding the massacre, and civil groups have advocated economic severance, but to completely resolve it, it is necessary to unite the strength of the whole country and work from the ground up. The basic work, first, is investigation and research, knowing yourself and your enemy, and you will win every battle. Second, is enrichment. As the saying goes, "Goods are hated when they are thrown on the ground," and "Careless storage invites thieves." Manchuria is one-third larger than Japan, and its population is two-thirds smaller than Japan. How can they not covet this when their country is suffering from overpopulation? The immigration of Zhejiang people to Heilongjiang the year before last failed due to differences in climate and customs. Now it is best to use a promotion method, such as moving Shandong people to Guanwai, moving Jiangbei people to Shandong, moving Jiangnan people and Zhejiang people to Jiangbei, and moving Minyue people to Jiangzhe. In the northwest, move Shaanxi and Gansu people to Xinjiang and Ningxia, and move Henan people to Shaanxi and Gansu, move Sichuan people to Kangzang, and move Huguang people to Sichuan. If handled properly, it is an important strategy for solving the problem of people's livelihood. If the three eastern provinces are enriched with Shandong people who are good at farming and business, and then the construction business is started with the strength of the whole country, then their aggressive plans, no matter how sophisticated and cunning, will be useless. At that time, if there are problems that are not easy to solve, we can use the Pan-Asianism principle to help them with friendship. The meeting adjourned at ten o'clock after the report.

▲ National Government: At 10:00 AM on the same morning, the National Government held a memorial week for the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen. Attendees included Yu Youren, Zhu Peide, Wang Boqun, Ma Fuxiang, Li Shuhua, Zhu Luhe, Lin Xiang, Ru Yuli, Chen Bulei, Chen Yi, Chen Shaokuan, Zhang Wohua, Wu Siyu, and over 300 staff from the National Government's civil affairs, military affairs, and accounting departments. Yu Youren chaired the meeting. After the salutations, Yu reported on the issue of suppressing communist bandits, roughly stating that he had recently received good news from the front that the anti-communist army had defeated the main force of the communist bandits, and their lairs had also been destroyed. The number of weapons seized was nearly 40,000. Although there is still a part of the communist bandits who are fleeing, the central army is blocking them from all sides, and it is expected that the communist bandits in Jiangxi can be completely resolved within a month. The reason for this victory in suppressing the communists is due to the efforts of all the soldiers and the help of the people. But the biggest reasons are: (1) The people hope that political construction and economic construction will be implemented one by one. The reason why they have not been implemented is because the communist bandits are a problem, so suppressing the communists is what the people most eagerly hope for. (2) The communist bandits burn and kill everywhere, digging their own graves. Our Three Principles of the People have deeply penetrated the hearts of the people. No matter how rampant heresy is, it cannot shake the hearts of the people. Therefore, wherever the central army goes, it has not failed. (3) The communist bandits propagate everywhere, saying how the people help the communist bandits. In fact, the people hate the communist bandits to the extreme. The reason why the communist bandits say this is to shake the hearts of the people. (4) This anti-communist work is extremely well-arranged. Whenever a place is recovered, all the party affairs and politics in that place can be handled with swift methods. (5) After the National Assembly, the Provisional Constitution was promulgated, and after the Fifth Plenary Session, the government was reorganized, completing the foundation of the party and government, which is unusually solid. Appropriate measures have been taken for party and government construction, so that rumor-mongers have no way to spread rumors, and those who slander the central government have no way to use their skills. With these several major reasons, the suppression of the communists has been victorious and can be completely resolved in the short term. However, after the victory in suppressing the communists, the people's hopes are very high, and international commentary is even stricter. This is what government colleagues should pay attention to. It is necessary to satisfy the people's hopes one by one, and also gain international sympathy, in order to seek China's freedom and equality in the international arena. Therefore, our future efforts are to satisfy the people's hopes. As for what the people hope for, it is nothing more than stability of life and the protection of property rights. However, these points cannot be achieved without true unification and peace in the country. When we read the chapter on people's livelihood in the Provisional Constitution, we should know that it is not easy to achieve. This is what government colleagues and the people should devote 120% of their efforts and the spirit of suppressing the communists to after the war, in order to have some success. Regarding the international aspect, Germany, after the European War, was oppressed too much by the Allied countries, and crises were everywhere. Recently, various countries, in view of the crisis in the Rhineland region of Germany, believe that in the current situation, it will either become communist or fascist. Therefore, various countries are making efforts to provide relief, so that Germany can overcome the crisis and maintain world peace. China's current situation is extremely unstable, and imperialists are deliberately creating trouble in China, creating opportunities for communist bandits, thinking that China's chaos is their benefit. But they do not know that the praying mantis stalks the cicada, unaware of the oriole behind. If the communist disaster spreads in China, the suffering of the imperialists will be even worse than that of China. It is deeply hoped that various countries will understand everything and give China sympathy. Now China is facing frequent internal and external troubles. The anti-communist military operations in Jiangxi have not ceased, and the tragic anti-Chinese massacre in Korea's Wanbaoshan is repeated. Everyone is heartbroken and demands that the government deal with it firmly. However, there are still unawakened military personnel in the country who plan to take advantage of the situation for their own benefit. It is said that there are white imperialists as the background, or that they are in contact with the Communist Party. Now that the communist bandits in Jiangxi are about to be wiped out, they have to rise up and support them. But in any case, there are many soldiers and officers in the north who understand the righteousness, and they will never be shaken by one or two who do not understand the righteousness. The current government has made all preparations for military affairs and will never relax the anti-communist military operations in Jiangxi because of the riots of one or two idle military personnel. These people, during the period of the large-scale anti-communist operations, rise up to disturb the people and help the communist bandits, which is not only harmful to the people, but also harmful to the country, and even more a crime against the international community. It is hoped that government colleagues will make up their minds to eliminate the traitors who aid communist bandits and disturb the local area, to remove the scourge of China for all ages, and to prevent the communist bandits who disrupt China and international peace from existing.

Severe Anti-Chinese Sentiment Among Koreans in Niigata Prefecture, Japan

▲ Over Ten Houses of Overseas Chinese Destroyed

▲ Thirteen Overseas Chinese Injured, One Abducted

Osaka Correspondence: Since the tragic massacre of overseas Chinese in Korea, it has gradually spread to the Japanese mainland. Incidents of Koreans attacking overseas Chinese, destroying their houses, and beating them have been reported in Osaka, Kobe, Kanazawa, Shizuoka, Toyama, and other places. Because the Japanese authorities do not seriously crack down on them, the anti-Chinese situation is becoming more widespread. On the 16th of this month, Korean laborers in Niigata Prefecture, Japan, suddenly gathered in large numbers, forming groups of hundreds, and attacked the overseas Chinese residing in the prefecture. More than ten houses of overseas Chinese near Naoe Town were destroyed, thirteen overseas Chinese were seriously injured, and Lin Zhengpu, an overseas Chinese, was abducted by the Koreans. The local Chinese association immediately telegraphed the embassy in Tokyo, requesting assistance in protecting them. The embassy, ​​due to its limited authority, was unable to do anything, so it telegraphed the Niigata Prefecture authorities, requesting them to take measures to crack down on the Koreans' atrocities and to effectively protect the lives and property of the overseas Chinese. Currently, most of the overseas Chinese in the area have taken refuge in nearby police stations. The Korean culprits arrested include Kim Cheong-fang and Yamamoto Kintaro. Furthermore, the Japanese side is not responsible for the medical expenses of the injured overseas Chinese and the losses from the destroyed houses. Negotiations between the consul and the Japanese authorities have also been ineffective. Therefore, the overseas Chinese all hope that our country's diplomatic authorities will also quickly lodge a serious protest against the anti-Chinese incidents by Koreans in the Japanese mainland, and demand compensation for the losses of the overseas Chinese. (July 17th)

Representatives of the Pyongyang Chinese Chamber of Commerce Appeal on Behalf of the Overseas Chinese

▲ Demand That the National Government Negotiate Five Items

To the National Government, the Central Party Headquarters, the Provincial Governments, the Provincial Party Headquarters, Overseas Compatriots, Newspapers, Societies, and Fellow Citizens: On the evening of the 5th of this month, Koreans suddenly launched a large-scale riot, forming teams and slaughtering overseas Chinese from house to house. Japanese police followed the rioters, without carrying weapons, in a state of secretly directing them. The intention is self-evident. The next day, the ferocity was even more intense. Goods were looted, and houses were completely demolished. Iron cabinets were placed on the streets and crushed with machines to take away the money. The ferocity soared to the sky, and the Japanese police saw it all, without any prevention. Approximately five hundred people died, and countless more were injured. Blood and flesh flew everywhere, and corpses piled up like mountains. Afterwards, the corpses were thrown into the Datong River or cremated. After two days, the Chinese were accommodated in a despicable place, which was like being under house arrest. It is estimated that there are more than 6,300 overseas Chinese near Pyongyang, who are lodging in the open air, with heavy rain pouring down. They cannot return, and they have nowhere to hide. Heads are broken and bleeding, and the sound of crying is endless. It's tragic! From the 12th to the 13th, they were gradually sent back to Luda via Zhennampo, without letting a single person return to Andong. This time, the property of our overseas Chinese merchants and households in Pyongyang and Hanchuan was completely destroyed and nothing was left. Several overseas Chinese compatriots in Hanchuan were also killed and injured. Our association secretly sent a person to escape to Andong alone today. We have already telegraphed our National Government to quickly send personnel to conduct a detailed investigation and serious negotiations. The conditions raised are as follows: (1) Compensation for losses, with a consolation payment of more than 5,000 yuan for each dead person. The rest of the losses, such as goods, etc., will be compensated in full after our government, together with the consuls of various countries, conducts a thorough investigation. (2) If the Japanese side does not provide a reliable guarantee, our country will send warships to be permanently stationed in the western Korean area. (3) Punish the instigators of the incident. (4) The Japanese must guarantee that such a tragedy will never happen again in the future. (5) If the negotiations are not satisfactory, immediately telegraph the whole country to sever economic relations with Japan. Overseas Chinese will return to their country in unison. Our association respectfully pleads for the lives of more than 6,000 overseas Chinese compatriots. It is urgent and we await orders. We hereby issue this special notice, and we earnestly request your association to publicize this vigorously for the sake of rescuing overseas Chinese compatriots and to act as a backing for the National Government, so that the negotiations will not fail and the remaining overseas Chinese will be able to celebrate their rebirth. Then the country will be fortunate, and the overseas Chinese will be fortunate. Please be informed. The Pyongyang Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Korea cries out, July 15th.

Rampant Resurgence of Local Bandits in Jiaodong

▲ Qingdao Municipal Government Plans Defensive Measures

Qingdao Correspondence: The bandits in various counties of Jiaodong were previously suppressed by the 25th and 58th Brigade Commanders Zhan Shutang, who sent troops to crack down on them. The bandit forces had temporarily subsided. Recently, due to the rising green screen, the bandit atmosphere has revived. The bandit gang in Xiaozhushan, Jiaoxian County, on the day after Commander Zhan returned to Wei, surrounded and attacked Xuejia Ridge Village for two days and nights due to unsuccessful extortion. They broke into the village, shooting and killing more than a hundred men, women, old and young. The entire village was reduced to ashes, and more than 600 houses were burned. In one family, not a single person survived, which was as cruel as the communist bandits. Recently, they have also sent people out to extort donations and, in order to replenish their strength, have set a deadline for handing over civilian self-defense firearms. More than a dozen guns from the Wanggezhuang militia were surrounded by bandits yesterday and all the guns were confiscated. Therefore, the bandits' power has recently increased. Furthermore, the local bandits in Zhucheng and Jiaoxian communicate with each other and are also very rampant. On the 13th of this month, forty bandits suddenly came to Xujiazhuang, fifteen miles south of the city, and kidnapped four students and one teacher from the village private school. Their whereabouts are still unknown. The authorities of Jiaoxian and Zhucheng counties have reported the bandit information to the provincial government and requested troops to suppress them. Furthermore, bandit alarms also frequently occur in the Haixi area of ​​this city due to its proximity to Xiaozhushan in Jiaoxian County. Villages such as Hao Cliff Village, Xindao Village, Liujia Island, Dongjiahe, Fenghuangshan, Tabutou, Hongshiya, and Xuejiadao have suffered repeatedly. At the beginning of this month, the Navy Headquarters sent warships and the Public Security Bureau Security Team to suppress them together. However, the bandits had already fled when they arrived. Each village had been looted by the bandits. The troops would leave when the bandits came, and the bandits would come when the troops left. The government troops could do nothing. The municipal government authorities are deeply afraid that this stalemate will continue and disturb the public security in the city. They have ordered the Public Security Bureau to plan preventive measures. The Public Security Bureau has decided to build a barracks in a suitable location in the Haixi area and station a company of the Security Team there permanently to deter them. (July 18th)

After the Communist Bandits Fled to Western Fujian

▲ Central Army Units Entering Fujian Make Rapid Progress

▲ Provincial Government Decides to Establish Relief Society for Communist Disaster Areas

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Central Army units entering Fujian to pursue the bandits have made rapid progress in recent days. Currently, Sun's division has advanced from Shaowu to Jiangle, Mao's division has also advanced from Jianning to Ninghua, and Liu and Lu's two divisions in Shunchang and Shaxian have also dispatched troops to attack on both sides. The communist bandits' pseudo-First Army Group, led by Zhu De, and the pseudo-Third Army Group, led by Peng Dehuai, totaling more than 20,000 people, have withdrawn from Jiangle and Ninghua and fled to Changting and Liancheng in western Fujian. According to reports, the bandits plan to retreat to Ruijin, Shicheng, and Ningdu in Jiangxi, and defend Changting, Liancheng, and Shanghang on the Fujian border for a final struggle. Currently, the anti-bandit troops of the two provinces are taking a large encirclement formation to completely wipe them out. The northern Fujian area has gradually become peaceful. However, after this great catastrophe, the counties of Chong'an, Guangze, Shaowu, Jiangle, Jianning, and Taining are in ruins, the people are displaced, and they are gathering in Jianyang, Jian'ou, Shunchang, and Yanping. They have sent representatives to the province to request relief from the provincial government. The provincial government held a special committee meeting on the afternoon of the 16th and decided to establish the Fujian Communist Disaster Area Relief Society, appointing Chen Peikun, Zheng Baojing, and Cheng Shikui as standing committee members. They first raised 6,000 yuan and sent personnel to Yan and Jian to handle urgent relief. Secondly, they organized a relief donation team for the communist disaster and conducted fundraising by region. The Fuzhou team is headed by Chairman Yang Shuzhuang as the chief commander, with thirty-two teams under it, headed by members of the provincial government, the provincial party headquarters, officials from the national tax authorities, military and police agencies, and major merchants. The Xiamen team is headed by Commander Lin Guogeng as the chief commander, with twenty teams under it. The Zhangzhou team is headed by Division Commander Zhang Zhen as the chief commander, with ten teams under it. The Shayong team is headed by Division Commander Lu Xingbang as the chief commander, with ten teams under it. The Quanzhou team is headed by Brigade Commander Chen Guohui as the chief commander, with ten teams under it. The Funing team is headed by Brigade Commander Jin Zhenzhong as the chief commander, with ten teams under it. The Xinghua team is headed by Commander He Xianzhu as the chief commander, with five teams under it. The chief commanders will appoint the team leaders themselves. The minimum donation amount for each team is 300 yuan. In addition, they will telegraph hometown associations in various ports to solicit donations and sponsorships. They can start the process within days. (July 17th)

Negotiations on Japanese Fishing in Shantou

▲ Over One Thousand Catties Intercepted by Customs, Fishing Boats Detained

Shantou Correspondence: Chaoshan has been affected by military affairs for many years. Chinese shipping companies' steamers have either been hired to carry soldiers and transport grain, or have been attacked and extorted by bandits, or have been forced to stop operating due to the inability to pay the shipping bureau's seasonal fees. The shipping situation has declined rapidly. Japanese Taiwanese electric boats have seized the opportunity to encroach on the inland river shipping industry. It is estimated that there are more than 30 Japanese small steamers and more than 10 Taiwanese small electric boats operating from Shantou to Zhao'an in Fujian and the coastal areas of Shanwei and Hailufeng, such as Jianxing, Wansheng, Wang'an, Anshun, Anqing, Qiteng, and Feipeng. The Japanese flag is often flown overseas in Shantou. As a result, Japanese fishing boats also often take the opportunity to mingle among them, such as the Gongxing Maru, Dongcheng Maru, and Baorong Maru, dozens of which often line up to fish in the Nanao Chaohu area and transport them to Shantou and Hong Kong for sale. Shantou fishermen have repeatedly appealed to the Construction Department to prohibit it. The Construction Department has ordered the Chaozhou Customs and the Maritime Administration Bureau to strictly investigate and deal with it. On the 6th, the Japanese fishing boat Gongxing Maru caught more than 1,000 catties of fresh fish outside Mayu in Shantou and transported it to Shantou for sale. It was discovered by the customs patrol boat, and the boat and fish were immediately detained. It is heard that the fish caught by the fishing boat the other day were transported to Shantou by sailing ships. On that day, due to the hot weather, the Maru was eager to send the fresh fish to the market, which led to its detention. Negotiations have already been initiated. (July 10th)

▲ Refugees Scattered Throughout Qingyuan and Sanshui

▲ Devastating Dyke Breaches and Losses in Various Areas

In Shantang Shengping Township's Rongshuwei embankment, there was a breach of over 150 zhang, inundating 1.5 million mu of rice fields and causing the collapse of over 200 houses. Qingyuan County Disaster Situation

▲ Xijiang Area (1) Sanshui: The disaster situation in Sanshui is the worst among the counties along the Xijiang River. The North District comprises 12 townships, situated on the east and west banks of the river. Five townships are on the east bank, and seven are on the west bank. The total population, male and female, in the district is over 50,000. On the east bank, the Dabuwei embankment had a breach of over 120 zhang, with a depth of over 2 zhang. In the above 12 townships, except for Ludong and Longtan, which were spared from inundation, all other townships were submerged in a vast flood. The water depth was 2 zhang in deep areas and 4 or 5 chi in shallower areas. Refugees were left homeless, awaiting relief. A total of over 240 houses, large and small, collapsed in the entire district, and over 700 mu of fields were submerged. In the South District, the Letangwei embankment, near Dushugang Village, with the local name Youyutian, breached 50 zhang on the 3rd of the month. All villages within the embankment were submerged, with water levels reaching 5 or 6 chi. A total of 71,000 mu of rice fields were affected in the entire district, with losses estimated at 710,000 yuan. The loss of rice seedlings and miscellaneous grains exceeded 230,000 yuan. In the Central District, the embankment breach areas included Langdong, Langxi, Lucun, Daliang, Gaofeng, and Shatou, totaling six townships. After the breaches, the water depth reached over 1 zhang, affecting over 30,000 refugees who were left homeless on the hills. (2) Sihui: The Mafang area of this county suffered the most severely. Soviet Union Establishes a Commercial Office in Liaoning

▲ Consul General Ci Speaks to Reporters

Shenyang Dispatch: The Soviet Union, in its business operations in the Northeast, aims for direct trade with Chinese merchants. It has already established the Soviet People's Foreign Trade Committee Representative Office in Harbin to handle commercial affairs in northern Manchuria. Recently, it also established a Soviet Commercial Office in Shenyang to handle commercial affairs in southern Manchuria, located in Maluwan, a commercial area. The manager is Zha Hareiji. The office has already started operations, contacting major Chinese commercial firms in Liaoning Province to discuss representation matters. Because the establishment of this commercial office within the Northeast involves trade issues, and the current state of Sino-Soviet talks seems impossible to ignore, this reporter visited the Soviet Consulate General in Liaoning to interview Consul General Ci Namin Siqi, who agreed to meet. The interview was translated by Secretary An Geliefu, and the following questions and answers were exchanged: (Question) I recently read foreign reports about the prohibition of buying and selling your country's goods in Liaoning, Harbin, and various parts of the Northeast. Is this true? (Answer) Currently, our country does not have much trade in China and the northeastern provinces. Everyone knows that our country's largest commercial transactions are with Germany, the United States, Italy, France, England, Turkey, Persia, and other countries. However, our country's commercial companies are also paying attention to trade with your country, because our country buys the most tea, furs, cotton, and other items from your country. The goods that our country sells to your country are only a portion of industrial and commercial products, such as kerosene and cloth. Regarding the prohibition of buying and selling Soviet goods in the Northeast, it has never happened before, and it certainly cannot happen now. (Question) Why can't there be a prohibition on trade with your country? The Sino-Soviet treaty of commerce has not yet been signed. Before a treaty is signed, naturally, there can be no trade. (Answer) The Sino-Soviet treaty of commerce has indeed not been signed, but the 1924 Beijing Agreement and the Fengtian-Soviet Agreement have mutually recognized the right to trade. The responsibility of the current Moscow Sino-Soviet Conference is to stipulate detailed methods for Sino-Soviet trade. If Soviet trade is prohibited now, it would be tantamount to rescinding the rights stipulated in our country's treaty with your country. (Question) According to your Consul General's opinion, the Chinese side cannot independently order the prohibition of your country's buying and selling and the establishment of companies in the Northeast? (Answer) This is not entirely true. Our country does not yet have a complete treaty of commerce with your country, because all of our country's previous old rights have been returned to China. The current commercial companies of our country must comply with your country's laws, regulations, and customs. If there are violations, such as buying and selling prohibited items or evading taxes, then the company bears a significant responsibility, and your country can certainly completely prohibit its business. (Question) How is your country's commercial office in Liaoning equipped, and what is its business policy? (Answer) This is very simple, because the office itself does not want to do business, but only wants to enter into contracts with reputable merchants in your country to buy goods on their behalf. Only a public affairs room, a goods display area, and a place for brokers to discuss business are sufficient. (Question) What are your country's goods prices and quality like? Is there any meaning to competitive sales? (Answer) The meaning of competitive sales is to transport many goods to foreign markets at a lower price than in the country, or even lower than the international average price. Selling goods in China is exceptionally cheaper than in other countries. This is competitive selling, used to disrupt the market, drive out other companies, and preserve one's own power. This is an act of attempted manipulation, but our country's commercial companies have a shallow history internationally and do not have many goods to transport abroad for competitive sales. Therefore, the term "competitive sales" should be removed from our country's trade, especially in China. In fact, there is no room for competitive sales, and our country does not directly sell goods in China, but entrusts Chinese merchants to sell them on our behalf, who will naturally sell at a profitable and appropriate price. According to my thinking, our country's companies and your country's merchants absolutely cannot voluntarily suffer losses. Since there is no power to manipulate the market, why sacrifice blood money in vain? (Question) How will your Consul eliminate the obstacles that arise during your country's trade? (Answer) There are no major obstacles. I said just now that the prohibition of selling Soviet goods cannot be implemented. Recently, no one has expressed a desire to destroy the Sino-Soviet Agreement, the Fengtian-Soviet Agreement, or the Boli Agreement. If our country's commercial companies have improper behavior, the scope of trade should be regulated. Our country's merchants do not demand special treatment, nor do they want to be treated particularly harshly. What is required is the right to equal status in accordance with the treaties established by both countries and the laws promulgated by China. (Question) I see that there is a case on the agenda of the Sino-Soviet Conference to establish a commercial treaty between the two parties. What is the situation of the conference? (Answer) The Sino-Soviet Conference is still continuing. Under the guidance of the talented and capable plenipotentiary Mo from your country, and with the substantial expressions that your country already has, naturally, a successful goal can be achieved. Currently, your country has other issues, so the conference has not been able to proceed actively. According to the news announced by your country, plenipotentiary Mo is working extremely hard to fulfill his mission completely, even in the sweltering summer, without rest, and plans to propose a detailed conference outline. The future can be optimistic. (July 14)

Local News

Changshu

The County Government Approves the Acceptance of the Party Committee's Accusation Case: Shi Minyong, the current supervisory committee member of the local county party headquarters, is accused in the Haiyu Daily of extorting Liu Bingshu of Shazhou City during the mediation of the San'gan River affair in 1928, and the correspondence is presented as evidence. Since this incident occurred, society has paid unusual attention. Subsequently, party member Tong Shizhong filed a complaint with the county government. It is now heard that after receiving the complaint, the county government issued a directive yesterday, ordering a summons for verification.

The Electric Light Company Will Voluntarily Reduce Prices: In order to increase power generation, the local electric plant specially ordered a diesel engine from abroad, which is currently being installed. As a result, the lights in half the city will be temporarily turned off for three weeks. However, electric light users and the company had previously signed an agreement last year, stating that the company would automatically reduce prices after the diesel engine was installed. According to the manager of the company, representatives elected by the users signed an agreement last year, but recently the price of diesel has soared, from 50 yuan per can to 90 yuan. However, in order to maintain credibility, the company decided to submit a proposal to the board of directors after the new engine is installed to voluntarily reduce prices, which will not exceed the Ministry of Communications' regulation of 25 cents.

The Battalion Requests Additional Garrison Troops, Temporarily Postponing Arrival in Changshu: The Second Battalion of the Changshu Provincial Security Force, originally stationed in Hupu by the Third Company and Sixth Company, the Fourth Company stationed in Taicang Fuqiao, and the Fifth Company still in Jiangyin, under the command of the regimental headquarters. Battalion Commander Guang, due to the insufficient number of soldiers in the battalion headquarters for deployment, specially submitted a request to the regimental headquarters to transfer the entire Fifth Company to Changshu for deployment, which was approved by the regimental headquarters. However, the day before, a company stationed in Pingwang suddenly mutinied. The Suzhou Command, therefore, telegraphed the Fifth Company of the Second Battalion stationed in Cheng to suppress the mutiny and guard the town. Therefore, the transfer to Changshu cannot be implemented temporarily.

Wuxi

Public Security Detectives Capture Three Thieves: Xue Furui, captain of the Public Security Bureau's detective team, received a confidential report on the 19th stating that several thieves who had robbed a family surnamed Mou near Qingqiao Bridge in Zhoujing Lane, Jingyun City, were hiding in Zhoushanbang in the Guangqin District and near Tingzi Bridge and Xiaomu Bridge outside the East Gate. After receiving the report, Captain Xue immediately led the informant and detectives such as Shen Dehua to search and arrest the thieves. At around 9 PM, three thieves were captured. Upon interrogation, one was from Tongzhou, one from Anhui, and one from Changzhou. According to Captain Xue's confession, a document was prepared and sent to the Public Security Bureau yesterday, while detectives were still dispatched in all directions to investigate the remaining accomplices. A Female Worker at a Yarn Factory Dies in a Tragic Accident: Ge Afeng, a 15-year-old female worker at the Zhenxin Yarn Factory in Taibodun outside the West Gate of the city, was from Site Tou Wangzhuang. On the 19th, Afeng went to the factory for the night shift. At around 1 AM yesterday, Afeng suddenly bent down to pick up a piece of yarn under the machine. Unexpectedly, her hair was caught in the roller, and in an instant, half of her head was crushed off, with blood flowing freely. She died shortly after. Seeing this, the female worker in the same car immediately instructed the driver to stop the car and pulled Afeng's body out from under the car, which was a bloody mess.

Two Robbery and Assault Cases Occur One After Another: Chen Chuande, the newly appointed county magistrate of the city, upon his arrival, immediately vowed to rectify and apprehend thieves. Unexpectedly, the wicked thieves still disregarded the law and acted recklessly. Yesterday, news came that two major robbery and assault cases occurred in the Second and Seventh Districts. They are recorded as follows: (1) In the Second District (Jingyun City), at the home of farmer Zhang Baoguan, near Baomiao Bridge, about four li from Houyangfang Qian, at around 11 PM on the previous day, more than ten thieves suddenly arrived, each wielding pistols, flashlights, and other weapons, speaking in a Jiangbei accent. They used a large stone to break open the front door and entered. One of the thieves fired a pistol shot to show their power. Unexpectedly, the bullet hit Baoguan's second son, Liansheng, in the left abdomen, piercing through to the right abdomen, causing profuse bleeding. He fell to the ground, barely breathing. Baoguan was also tied up with ropes by the thieves, who forced him to reveal the location of the hidden silver. Subsequently, they went from room to room, overturning boxes and chests, and searching arbitrarily. At that time, the sound of gongs rose up, and the thieves, realizing that things were not going well, immediately fled with their stolen goods. After inspection, it was estimated that the stolen cash and clothes were worth about 100 yuan. Yesterday, Zhang Baoguan rushed his injured son to the city by boat and took him to Pu Ren Hospital for treatment. His life is expected to be spared. (2) In the Seventh District (Huai Shang City), at the home of villager Fang Jisheng in Jintou Shang, eight or nine thieves also broke into the house the night before, immediately seizing Li, Jisheng's concubine, and placing a Mobil oil lamp in the toilet, forcing Li to sit down naked and whipping her, causing her vagina to be scalded beyond recognition. Fang Ziyingkui was also beaten and injured by the thieves. Another three thieves entered the room to search, stealing more than 300 yuan in cash, as well as gold and silver jewelry, clothes, and other items, totaling more than 600 yuan in losses.

Torrential Rain Damages Famous Scenic Spots and Historical Sites: Zhenjiang has been experiencing continuous torrential rain recently, causing great losses to crops. Also, the retaining wall of Elephant Mountain was damaged by falling stones. Fortunately, there was no major damage, but if repairs are not carried out as soon as possible, tourists will find it very inconvenient.

Yangzhou

A Tragic Live Burial Occurs in Qianjiashan: Qianjiashan, about ten li from the city in the west, has a fierce public sentiment and is accustomed to harboring bandits. Police detectives dare not intervene. At 10 AM on the 13th, Qian Sanxi's son, Yu Dahualian, and Xue Youfu went to Xue Yougui's house. One person guarded the door, and two people climbed over the wall and entered, using a rope to strangle Yougui on the bed and carrying him to a pre-dug pit. While he was still breathing, they covered him with a dustpan, trampled on his feet for a long time, and covered him with soil. At that time, the deceased's eldest son, Xiao Wenzhai (age 13), followed and saw the situation and cried loudly. Qian and others ran away. The neighborhood chief Wang Gui reported to the Situ Temple Public Security Patrol Rest Station, and Patrol Chief Dai sent police to investigate. The murderers shouted for them to be tied up. Director Chen Yueqiao dissuaded them. The next morning, the neighborhood chief reported to the Tenth Branch of the Public Security Bureau again. The murderers gathered a crowd at the bureau, falsely claiming that the deceased was colluding with bandits and had been executed by public anger, asking for the case not to be reported. It is heard that the deceased's wife, Qian, is working in Shanghai and has three children, who are now being taken care of by the deceased's father-in-law, Qian Lao Mizi. It is also heard that the deceased left behind six or seven mu of high-yielding fields and a house, which he sold to Li Zhicheng last year, with 70 yuan still owed. Recently, he urged for payment, which led to this tragedy.

Nantong

County Magistrate Zhang specially convened the district chiefs of the entire county and representatives of various agencies to discuss the method of funding and immediately began preparations. The coastal anti-piracy water special team must still be combined with Rugao, Hai'an, and Dongtai counties to form a group.

The Additional Collection of Land Tax to Support Bank Erosion Mitigation: Tongyi's coastal areas are carrying out bank erosion mitigation projects. The Provincial Government has agreed to allocate funds for subsidies. The local funds are currently being approved by the Provincial Government to collect an additional bank erosion mitigation tax of 3.5 cents per mu of land, estimated to be collected for five years, which can yield 200,000 yuan.

Investigation and Prohibition of Self-Funded District Expenses: The Department of Civil Affairs learned that the district offices in Nantong often temporarily raised funds on the spot to compensate for insufficient funds, causing many malpractices. The Department specially ordered the county government to properly allocate and control all district administrative expenses and district business expenses from the county allocation of funds and the district's inherent income, and strictly prohibit unauthorized fundraising.

Qingjiang

Hui Zhi Records of Bandit News in Huai and Si: (1) Since the execution of bandit Ding Qifeng in Yugou Town, Huaiyin at the beginning of the month, Ding's followers, numbering over a hundred, have been spreading rumors that they will slaughter the entire town of Yugou to take revenge. As a result, merchants and residents of the town have been fleeing every night since the 5th of the month, with the sound of cranes and the wind causing panic every night. On the evening of the 12th, people fled in the rain, and two mothers of Ding Chengyi and Ju Qiyou, and two daughters of Liu Wanyou, accidentally fell into the water and drowned. On the 14th, over one hundred male and female representatives of the town's residents, including Wu Qiqing, came to the city to petition the county government and the 25th Route General Headquarters. General Liang has already allocated two companies of infantry from an independent brigade stationed in Yangjiazhuang to suppress the situation. (2) County Magistrate He received a report from Zhang Yaosong, the director of the Second Branch of the Matou Public Security Bureau, stating that there are two groups of bandits in the lakeside area of the Second District, Wei Yousan and Li Erxiansheng, numbering about a thousand or more, currently causing trouble in Xiaowuji, Shunheji, Chenji, and Xiaoqiao. The bandits are divided into two types: plainclothes and armed, making it difficult to distinguish between good and bad villagers. According to the report, He has telegraphed County Magistrate Wen Qinming of Siyang, and both parties will carry out a joint suppression. He has also telegraphed the provincial government to request that it consult the Anhui Provincial authorities and order the magistrates of Quyi and Sixian to cooperate in the suppression. (3) When it rained heavily on the night of the 12th in Wangyi, Linyi, and Luyi in Siyang, they were suddenly attacked and breached by two groups of bandits, Zuo Liangfeng and Huang Degui, who killed four villagers. They then attacked the Xu family in Wangzhuang, and the situation was critical. Township Chief Shan Taicui and Shan Yangqing of Shanwei Township telegraphed the Siyang garrison, and Brigade Commander Liu Guoming ordered Regiment Commander Wang Dehong to lead two platoons of soldiers to rescue them. It is now heard that the bandits have been defeated.

Hangzhou

Three Lives Lost for Twenty-Four Yuan: A county-owned Sandun-bound boat sailing on the Wan'an Bridge in Hangzhou struck and sank a civilian boat a few days ago in that town. A farmer named Zhu Zihe, 28 years old, fell into the lake and drowned. A local wealthy merchant, Xu Taihe, mediated, instructing the boat owner, Zhou Rongzhao, to give the deceased's father twenty-four yuan as compensation for funeral expenses. Unexpectedly, the father returned home with the money and recounted the event. His daughter-in-law, who was pregnant, was greatly grieved upon hearing the news and injured herself in a fit of despair. She also died the next day, a truly tragic event.

Woman Sold into Prostitution Escorted to Court: Shen Shao, the 21-year-old wife of farmer Shen Ziyan from Qingshi Bridge, Linping, ran away from home due to discord with her husband. She went to a relative's house in the upper four villages and was lured by Shen Dongfa, a barber from a nearby area. Yesterday, she was abducted to Hangzhou with the intention of being sold to Shanghai. However, her husband happened to be searching for her and spotted her on Pinghai Road. He immediately seized her and handed her over to the police station, who then transferred her to the court for detention. He also filed a criminal complaint.

End of Clean-Up Operations in Zhejiang Province: The Zhejiang Provincial Clean-Up Bureau was established on March 25th, with corresponding bureaus set up in various cities and counties. The positions of Director and Deputy Director were concurrently held by Provincial Chairman Zhang Nanxian and Committee Member Fang Ce, and the work was quite active. However, due to the difficulty of completing the household registration survey within the three-month deadline, the provincial government decided to extend the deadline by one month. Now that the work is gradually being completed, it has been decided to abolish all items by July 31st and hand over the handling of various cases to the Security Office and the court. It was heard yesterday that the winding down has already begun.

Liaoning Education Statistics

▲Universities: 4... Middle Schools: 271... Elementary Schools: 10,129

丨Total Private Funding for the Province: 3,819,011 Yuan

Shenyang Correspondence: Liaoning is a vast and resource-rich province, possessing 1,154,073 square li of fertile land and over 16 million outstanding people. In recent years, due to oppression by Japanese imperialists, the Chinese people have become increasingly determined. They deeply understand that to save China, education is essential. First, Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang generously donated 5 million yuan of his private funds to be used as a foundation for improving primary and secondary school education, in order to promote education. As a result, education has flourished and made daily progress. Recently, national attention has shifted to the Northeast. No fewer than hundreds of organized tours come to Shenyang each year to investigate, demonstrating the importance placed on it. This is especially true for the Japanese. Below is a detailed overview of the state of education in the province from 1919 to the end of June this year, which I believe will be welcomed by those concerned about education in the Northeast.

Fujian Education Department Summer School Opening Ceremony

The Fujian Education Department is running its third summer school to enhance the knowledge of educational personnel. Over 460 people have registered, representing 41 counties. Nineteen scholars from within China have been hired, including Li Shicen, Chen Heqin, Zheng Tonghe, Xia Chengfeng, Du Zozhou, Cheng Maojun, and Ma Ketan. There are a total of 22 courses. The opening ceremony was held on July 15th in the auditorium of the Education Department. In addition to all the students, more than 10 representatives from the party and government, including Lin Zhiyuan, Xu Xianshi, Gan Yun, and lecturers Cheng Maojun and Du Zozhou, were present. The ceremony began with a report from Director Cheng, the chairman, on the preparations for the summer school and the number of students in each subject. He then clarified the three points of significance in running the summer school: 1. To take advantage of the summer vacation to improve the ability of educational personnel to run schools; 2. To cultivate the spirit of learning among educational personnel; 3. To create a good atmosphere for learning in the educational sector. This was followed by speeches from party and government representatives Gan Yun and Chen Shoufan. Next, lecturer Cheng Maojun sang a famous song, followed by a lecture by lecturer Zozhou, entitled "The Contradiction Between Modern Chinese Educational Theory and Practice."

Curriculum Standards Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools Holds General Meeting

The primary school group meeting yesterday discussed the general outline today.

Revisions made to graduation limits for art and music.

Nanjing, 20th - The Primary School Group of the Curriculum Standards Compilation Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools held its second general meeting at the Ministry of Education on the morning of the 20th. The chairman was Gu Shusen. The following was resolved: (1) The three subjects of National Language, Health, and Society, in addition to being passed according to the revised opinions of the previous review committee, will have review committee members appointed to hold meetings in three groups on the morning of the 21st. The National Language group will be chaired by Wu Yan Yin, the Health group by Ma Ketan, and the Society group by Jiang Xicen. (2) The three courses of Nature, Labor, and Kindergarten will be passed in accordance with the amended proposals of the review committee. (3) Arithmetic, except for the operational items of the abacus, which will be amended, will be passed according to the review. (4) The graduation limit for fine arts at the primary level will be changed to "being able to explain the meaning of a picture depicting ordinary events, and being able to sketch simple landscapes without major errors." The graduation limit for the advanced level will be "being able to sketch objects without major errors, and being able to use natural objects to create patterns and simple quick successive drawings." (5) The minimum graduation limit for music at the primary level will be changed to "being able to sight-sing C major single-note songs," and the minimum graduation limit for the advanced level will be changed to "being able to sight-sing

C major single-note songs." The rest will be passed according to the review proposal. (6) The general outline of the curriculum will be discussed at the general meeting on the afternoon of the 21st.

Chang Qiaojiyuan has submitted his resignation and requested compensation for accumulated arrears. Great Britain Upset the United States in the Davis Cup Interzone Final

▲Great Britain Wins 3-2

丨Great Britain's Eleven-Year Wish Fulfilled丨

丨United States Loses After Leading Due to Failure in Three Singles Matches丨

▲Great Britain to Face France in Final Starting on the 24th

▲Paris dispatch - The United States had participated in every Davis Cup tennis competition since 1919. However, in this competition, full of hope, a bolt from the blue shattered the dreams of the American tennis world. The bad news of the American team's 2-3 defeat spread to all five continents. Today, the United States is hanging its head in sorrow, while Great Britain is triumphant. Great Britain has always regarded tennis as a national sport, but after being defeated by the United States in the final eleven years ago, its reputation declined and it was forced to submit to others. However, its ambition to rise again has never been forgotten. As heroes create opportunities, Great Britain has managed to defeat the United States 3-2 today to fulfill its long-cherished wish. However, the ultimate goal is to defeat France and win the championship. This is just a small test of its skills.

▲Complete Results of the Great Britain-United States Interzone Final

Austin (GB) (2 6 6 0 8 6 7 5) d. Wood (US)

Shields (US) (10 8 6 4 6 2) d. Perry (GB)

Van Ryn & Lott (US) (6 1 6 4 4 6 6 3) d. Hughes & Perry (GB)

Perry (GB) (6 3 8 10 6 3 6 3) d. Wood (US)

Austin (GB) (8 6 6 3 7 5) d. Shields (US)

▲Sudden Turnaround in the Final Act

In the first two singles matches, Great Britain and the United States each won one. At that time, British opinion was that Great Britain had returned to its former golden age. The United States won the doubles match the next day, taking a 2-1 lead. As a result, the American side was preparing to sing a triumphant song to celebrate the success of its young players. The British hope did not diminish, and they still believed that hard work would lead to success. In the final act, the situation suddenly changed. Both British singles players won, gaining the right to decide the championship. From now on, Great Britain will take a step forward in the hope of defeating France and winning the Davis Cup.

▲Rising Rapidly, Heroes Succeed

Since Great Britain won the Davis Cup in 1912, it fell into the hands of the United States and France the following year, becoming something that could be hoped for but not achieved. Since the arrival of this year's representatives Austin, Perry, and Hughes, they have defeated Morocco, retired from South Africa, defeated Japan, overcome Czechoslovakia, and upset the United States, rising rapidly. The fate of their final success will be decided in the Great Britain-France final on the 24th, 25th, and 26th of this month. The coach of this year's British team is Brett, a 57-year-old tennis veteran. His war history is worth recalling. Thirty-one years ago, Brett partnered with Black to represent Great Britain in the first Davis Cup match against the United States in Boston. As a result, they were defeated by the Americans Ward and Davis. Davis is the owner of the Davis Cup that is now famous all over the world, and also the Governor-General of the Philippines. With the guidance of the experienced Pao, the three British heroes should have today's excellent results. According to tennis experts, the French players are not in a good situation this year, and Great Britain has a bright future.
