Words of Insight

— Yimei

▲A wife's nagging and reproach are the most heartbreaking. Being in such a family is like falling into the Avici Hell.

▲To avoid humiliation, desire little. To desire little, endure hardship.

▲Rain threads cannot be used as clothing; dew drops cannot be used as adornment.

▲Beauty pageants are the precursors to nude parades.

▲Saturday night is the happiest time of the week.

▲When reading travelogues, it is best to open the window early in the morning. When reading biographies of beauties, it is best to close the door in the quiet of the night.

▲Those who charge by the word for manuscripts rarely produce good work. Those who write by the word rarely produce good essays.

▲Poems should be recited casually. Once you try to make them, they become vulgar. Paintings should be done casually. One stroke and they enter the path of evil.

▲Scholars of old lamented the shortness of the day. Today's students also lament the shortness of the day, but what they lament is Sunday.

▲An abundance of words and intricacy of meaning in late-life writings are signs of longevity.

▲Passing by a cosmetics store, I feel nothing towards the fragrances of powders and perfumes. But once a beauty uses them to adorn herself, the fragrant air that spreads on the wind is enough to stir up fantasies, making one feel like dying or becoming an immortal.

▲Ancient ballads conveyed meaning and lament. Today's ballads serve as propaganda.

▲The bored me is accustomed to doing boring things and good at making boring remarks.

Six Weeks of Living Under Snow

— Yang Moyi

On December 6th of last year, British explorer Ackley Grantaire joined the British Arctic expedition. He flew to Greenland for exploration, and after the expedition, everyone except him returned to their starting point. He was the only one who volunteered to stay there for the winter, hoping for new discoveries.

Unexpectedly, on January 4th, the sky suddenly filled with dark clouds, and goose-feather-like snowflakes began to fall. Overnight, his door was completely blocked by snow, making it impossible to enter or exit. He then opened another hole in the roof as a door for entering and exiting. But by March 18th, this hole, which he relied on to enter, was also blocked by snow and ice. He had to open another hole, but the snow kept falling, and it became heavier every day. Snowflakes danced in the roaring northwest wind, as if millions of jade dragons were fiercely fighting. So, in less than three days (March 21st), he was completely buried under the snow.

His relatives and friends did not receive any news from him for a long time. In early April, they organized a rescue team to look for him, but failed. On April 20th, Huajinsi organized another team to search, but they were also very disappointed. Because when they arrived in Greenland, all they could see was a snow-white and flawless silver world, and they could not find any information about Grantaire. After searching for more than ten days, they accidentally saw two flagpoles and the tips of air pipes slightly exposed on the snow surface from the plane. So they stationed at the ice corner and shouted loudly by the air pipes. Grantaire also cheered and responded from below. On May 5th, they dug out Grantaire, who had been buried in the snow for six weeks, from the snow cave more than three meters deep. He was safe and sound, and as healthy as ever. Although he had lived like a prisoner for six weeks, they did not return from Greenland until the 11th...

According to Grantaire, "Since I was completely buried underground on March 21st, I didn't feel any danger.

I had wine to drink, cigars to smoke, and interesting novels to pass the time, so I didn't worry about anything. But when the last candle cast its last light on me, I lay in the dark all day and felt something was wrong. But what could I do? I could only resign myself... On May 5th, when I was getting impatient, I suddenly heard a sound above my head that was as noisy as a fight during a football game. I was startled by it and immediately roused all my spirits. I also heard someone shouting very clearly, 'Hey, are you okay? We have started working to rescue you.' Ah, this was really unexpected luck! To be blunt, I thought that in this desperate situation, no one could save me, and I planned to wait for death to cruelly announce my end, which would be refreshing. So when I suddenly heard that someone was coming to save me, I was immediately overjoyed and cheered uncontrollably. And I will tell you a funny thing, that from the time I was buried under the snow until I was rescued, during these very long six weeks, I never left my cigar for a moment. I always smoked madly, as if I would die immediately if I left the cigar..."

Returning from the Pinghan Railway

— Jiguan

My friend Mr. Gu has just returned from the Pinghan Railway to the Longhai Railway, covered in dust. He told me about the current situation of the Pinghan Railway. According to him, China's railways have been affected by military affairs over the years, and the Pinghan Railway has suffered the most severe losses. Now that the situation is generally stable, passenger transport has not yet returned to its original state. Travelers on this route often experience unusual hardships.

The railway has always relied on freight transport as its main source of income. Among the stations along the way, Zhengzhou is the most important point on the entire line. The products of the northwestern provinces mostly pass through here. In the past two years, commerce has greatly decreased, and there has been little transshipment. With insufficient freight, passenger tickets have also been reduced accordingly. The reason for this is the extraordinary increase in disaster victims, coupled with a shortage of vehicles, resulting in this phenomenon. Currently, there is one special express train departing from Beijing to Hankou every day. Because it does not stop at small stations in between and has military police checking on board, passengers are not too crowded. However, the carriages are mostly old and dilapidated, far inferior to the Jinpu Railway, let alone the Huning Railway. And the pulling power of the locomotives is insufficient, so they cannot arrive on time. As for ordinary trains or intercity trains, they are often either open wagons or suffocating cars. Passengers are packed like sardines, and lice are everywhere, no different from a prison. When there is not enough space, people also sit on the roof of the car. The scorching sun steams, and sweat pours down like rain, but they don't care. The departure time is often uncertain. There are times when the scheduled time is in the morning, but it arrives more than ten hours late. Passengers who bought tickets often argue, but there is nothing they can do. According to people in the railway bureau, military vehicles are congested along the way, and they must give way to the tracks, so there is no way to clear the traffic.

My friend suffered greatly on his journey from Beijing to Shijiazhuang. He said that when the carriages were crowded, he had to sit sideways in between, and even urination was not free. Women found it especially difficult and often frowned. Therefore, some women carry several empty cans when taking ordinary trains. When they feel the urge to urinate, they sneak into their pants and use them as a means of excretion. After finishing, they cover the cans and throw them out of the car. Although it is inevitable that there will be some leakage, it is still a way to deal with the emergency. Mr. Gu witnessed this and found it very strange.

Record of the Fan Fair of Celebrities in Suzhou and Shanghai

— Zhu 

Mr. Liu Junran, a famous painter in Suzhou, once studied with the old painter Mr. Chen Jianan. He is skilled in painting and thoroughly studies the six principles of painting. His works of flowers, birds, insects, and fish are elegant and overflowing with beauty, making him a master in his own right. Seeing the repeated disasters in various places, he was deeply moved. Therefore, he and Mr. Chen Jianan and Mr. Zhang Junliang initiated the Fan Fair of Calligraphy and Painting by Famous Artists in Suzhou and Shanghai. The proceeds from the sale, after deducting expenses, were all used for charitable purposes. It has been open to the public for exhibition at Lejun Society in Gongxiang, Suzhou, since the 13th. Famous paintings and calligraphy are dazzling, how can it not be recorded?

Liu Linchuan, Yan Chunsheng, and Jiang Yian are the three elders of the painting circle in Suzhou. Their paintings all have an ancient feel. However, they are all nearing their seventies and are reluctant to use ink. However, they all have works on display at this fan fair. Liu Linchuan's landscapes are elegant and vast, deeply embodying the essence of Shigu. Yan Chunsheng's picture of Zhong Kui holding an umbrella and lantern, stumbling and wandering, vividly depicts the frustrated state of life, and he wrote a poem to record it: "Not riding a fine horse, not taking a carriage, rain dripping on clothes, sweat dripping on beard. Clouds and trees are vast, lanterns are dim, waking up at night, I fear ghosts laughing." It is especially filled with emotion. Jiang Yian's figures are leisurely and far-reaching, deeply entering the realm of Xiaolou. Mr. Chen Jianan has always presented his works in an old and vigorous style. This time, in the painting exhibition, he painted a lady, graceful in the wind, with a unique charm and beauty, which is especially refreshing. And Mr. Liu Junran's works, melons, fruits, fish, and birds, use a unique brushwork, further adding color to the exhibition. In addition, the calligraphy of Zhang Zhonglao, Li Yinquan, and Jiang Yinqiu, and the paintings of Gu Moyi, Fan Shaoyun, and Ma Wanli are also rare works. And the senior Mr. Cheng Xiaoqing also painted a Fish Joy picture in his busy schedule. So many famous works, it is truly a grand gathering in the art world. The fans in the painting exhibition are numbered according to the fan. Each ticket costs one and a half yuan, and there are first, second, and third prizes. Each prize is given four fans. The lottery will be drawn in public on the morning of the 15th. The fluttering of skirts and fans was especially lively.

Letter

Dear reporter, the reprint of manuscripts is permitted by law, but from a moral point of view, at least the source and the author's name should be indicated to avoid accusations of plagiarism. Now, a well-known domestic publication, such as "Guowen Zhoukan," has reprinted an article published in "Free Talk" (November 6th, 19th year, "Scraps of Political Sea") in its entirety, without changing a word. For example, the article "Cook Cao" appeared in the 25th issue of the 8th volume of the newspaper. Not only was the source not indicated, but the original signature UB was changed to "Lvyang Kanshang Sanren." This kind of behavior of plagiarizing other people's works as one's own is very immoral. Whether there is such a person as "Lvyang Kanshang Sanren" in the world is unknown, but the editor of "Guowen Zhoukan" should bear considerable responsibility. This is entirely a moral responsibility, because if it is not discovered by myself, people will suspect that I have submitted one manuscript to two places. Please publish this letter on my behalf as a statement. Brother WUB.

Travels in India (64)

— Linghua

On the 27th, teacher Sharma Nanada told me about Gandhi's movement, saying that Gandhi had deeply understood and applied Buddhist psychology. Gandhi had traveled to various Buddhist places and practiced the Buddhist principle of non-killing. If someone hit a snake, Gandhi would not approve of it because it was also created by God. Gandhi said that if someone insulted his wife, he would not retaliate, but only ask God to enlighten him. Although Gandhi studied in England, he did not use English knowledge, but invented Indian psychological affairs, the spirit of Mahavira's fearlessness, and unanimously refused to buy British goods. The British were starving to death. They unanimously resisted taxes, and the British were fined beyond their ability to pay, and they had no money to support their troops. The foundation of the government was shaken. According to me, Gandhi's movement is an anarchist movement. The masses rise up to resist taxes, how can the government exist? But I don't understand why the government has no legal means to deal with it. Many Indians told me that in this way, the British could kill them as they pleased without resistance, just by not paying taxes. Not handing over money is like being able to lead an ox to the water's edge but not being able to force it to drink. It is using the psychology of inertia. Students often regard Gandhi as a god, and Westerners also respect and believe in him. He has just been released from prison and is holding a large meeting to see the British Governor. It can be said that the three Su have returned to the court.

There are Nepalese students in Indian schools who advised me to visit their country. Nepalese people are fair-skinned and different from Indians. They said that their country has a Mongolian race, which is close to the Chinese race. Indians also said that the Nepalese race is close to the Mongolian race. They said that there are tens of thousands of Nepalese people in this city. Nepal is a purely Buddhist country. Their father is the army chief of the country, and their uncle once paid tribute to China. He is eighty years old this year and can speak Chinese. He is still learning Chinese and has been in China for two years. From Nepal to China, they did not go through India in the past, but went east through the snow-capped mountains. It took two years for a round trip and tribute was paid every three years. They said that it takes only two days to get from this place, Varanasi, to Nepal, and the place is quite cold, near the snow-capped mountains. Monk Jie Fa has visited it and said that there are many Avalokitesvara Bodhisattva statues there, which he has not seen in India.

The professors told me that India is now determined to revive its culture and does not stick to the old ways of the past, but imitates the great revolutions in various fields and strives to create with scientific methods, and must not be revived only in the world. They are willing to keep me here as a home to engage in the unity of all Asia. I greatly admire their arguments and feel their high regard. In short, Varanasi is the center of ancient Indian culture. People's hearts are deeply rooted in culture, even more than in Calcutta. They do not attach much importance to the importance of Calcutta in Indian culture. Generally speaking, India's knowledge and morality in philosophy, religion, and life are far richer than the money of the United States today. In the United States, selecting a lower-class capitalist can be upper-class in various countries. This is material wealth. In India, selecting a lower-class philosopher or intellectual and traveling around the world is still enough to be the king of philosophy and religion. Therefore, it is said that Buddhist wisdom is like the sea. In fact, Buddha is only one fruit of India, and the Indian people are the whole tree of wisdom.

Fiction Rotary Club

??? (27)

— Xu Zhuodai

So the nanny went downstairs again to get a pair of bowls and chopsticks. Ziliang sat on a small stool in front of the bed and used the rice plate as a table to eat with his wife. Ziliang originally didn't want to eat porridge; but if he ate rice that was different from what his wife ate, his wife would have more to say. So he had to make do with eating it. That night, his wife ate a lot of porridge, a total of five bowls, while Ziliang only ate two bowls.

After eating, Ziliang thought about going to the pavilion; however, he knew that tonight, because of the white ghost issue, he might not be able to leave for half a step.

Porridge is ultimately made of water. After his wife ate five bowls, her stomach naturally swelled and she had to go behind the bed to go to the toilet. Ziliang took this opportunity to try to get away:

"It stinks! I'm going to the pavilion!"

"No! I'm scared alone!"

Ziliang couldn't move an inch and had to endure the smell. When his wife returned to bed:

"It's so cold and quiet, too lonely! Tell me a joke!"

Ziliang was extremely flustered, how could he think of any joke?

"Jokes need a trigger, I can't think of one right now."

"Then, look in the first drawer, what books are there?"

Ziliang searched in the drawer and found three or four books:

"Do you want to read them?"

"Tell me first, what books are they?"

"Arabian Nights."

"Oh! I'm so scared! I don't want it!"

"How about reading Romance of the Three Kingdoms?"

"Good!"

Wheat Market Oscillates with an Upward Trend

▲Rumor that Russian Wheat Samples Have Been Sent to Shanghai

Yesterday's wheat market was supported by the persistently firm sentiment in the hinterland due to flooding in various regions. Some shorts slightly covered their positions due to the tight market situation, so the prices for all months showed a slight upward trend in the midst of oscillation. However, there were rumors in the market that samples of Russian wheat had been sent to Shanghai and were being actively offered. Whether this is true will be confirmed later. Silk and Tea: Factory Transactions with the US Have Stalled

Factory transactions of Shanghai white silk with the United States have been stagnant for a long time. Silk weaving factories in New York and other ports have uniformly suspended summer vacations due to unusually hot weather after the start of summer. There is a market for raw silk but no transactions. Silk telegrams were still not moving yesterday. Sales to the UK and France are also light. Yesterday, only Taihe shipped ten packages of Shanghai white factory silk to Shanghai, Xinfu shipped five packages of yellow factory silk, and Dachang shipped ten packages of white dry silk. The prices were all firm.

Fifty Loads of New Summer Cocoons Have Arrived in Wuxi

This year's summer silkworm crop in the various districts of Wuxi suffered damage from fertilizer and weather, resulting in a surprisingly poor harvest. The output of cocoons in various urban and rural areas is almost zero. Few cocoon firms have opened, and there is almost no cocoon market to speak of. The receipts of each firm are only about 30% of the spring cocoons. The cocoon market closed early. Fifty loads of new summer dried cocoons were shipped to Shanghai yesterday, consisting of goods from Henglin and Bashiqiao. They have now been placed in warehouses awaiting sale.

Uncolored High-Grade Tea Trade Active with US

Yesterday, in the Shanghai tea market for foreign firms, Jinjiang Foreign Firm, which handles high-grade uncolored tea from the Pingshui and Luzhuang roads, increased its intention to purchase due to telegrams from abroad requesting more. A total of more than 4,000 boxes were sold in the city at a price of 57-58 taels, unchanged from before. Ordinary goods from Wuyuan and Tunxi remain sluggish.

North-South Goods: Price of Green Bamboo Shoots Has Become Cheap

Since the introduction of green bamboo shoots, the supply has been abundant, and buyers have been cautious and made few purchases. Therefore, sellers had to gradually lower prices in order to accommodate buyers. Currently, high-quality "shang-shang-tu-ting" goods are selling for about 7 qian per catty, which is a low price compared to the usual market price. It is also said that the inventory at the origin is almost exhausted, and mountain traders are suffering losses and unwilling to sell cheaply, so it is expected that prices will be difficult to lower further and may even rebound.

Sugar Market: Sales of Japanese Sugar Halted Starting Today

▲Taikoo Sugar Opens Higher and is Snappy

Yesterday, no telegrams arrived from the sugar-producing areas. The price of Dutch 24 grade coarse granulated sugar at the guild market was quite firm, and supply was very tight, with prices quoted at 11.5 taels. However, a few sales at that price were made at the quoted price of 11 taels, 4 qian, and 2.5 fen. The market shape was very firm. Grade 20 medium granulated white sugar was 11 taels, with quieter demand. Taikoo Sugar spot goods grade B were priced at 11 taels, grade HM at 11 taels and 3 qian, and grade H at 10 taels and 6 qian. The market was snappy. The company offered 5,000 bags of grade DY August futures yesterday at a price of 4.85 yuan per day, and grade B at 5.05 yuan. In the afternoon, more than 2,000 additional bags were offered, and the price rose another 0.05 yuan. The momentum for price increases seems to be continuing. Sales of Japanese sugar have no room to move due to the boycott, so merchants are willing to cut prices to sell off their inventory, resulting in a sharp decline. Grade N sugar was 11 taels, 1 qian, and 5 fen to 0.05 yuan; Grade YT was 11 taels, 1 qian to 11 taels; Grade YR0 was 10 taels and 9 qian, with the lowest being 0.08 yuan; Grade TM was 10 taels; Grade TX was 11 taels, 3 qian to 2.5 qian; Grade YP was 11 taels, 5 qian, and 5 fen to 3.5 qian; Grade AE was 11 taels and 4 qian. The market was weak. In addition, the industry association convened a general meeting of its members and, in the name of economic severance with Japan, implemented a halt to trading in Japanese sugar on the market starting today. In addition, Zhenxiang Trading Company sold 1,000 bags of spot coarse granulated white sugar at the quoted price of 11 taels, 4 qian, and 2.5 fen. The market was quite snappy and had the potential to rise further.

Oil Market: Tung Oil Sales in Hongjiang Are Starting to Pick Up

The current period is the season for sales of tung oil from Hongjiang. Although sales may be brisk during the spring, this is mainly due to merchants stocking up. The summer season is when it is actually put to use.

Recently, the weather has been unsettled, resembling the plum rain season. However, the weather is gradually getting hotter, and the sun is unyielding. Farmers, having finished planting, are enjoying both rain and sunshine. If there is nothing to do on the ridges, they can engage in painting with lacquer. Therefore, the sales of oil are gradually starting to pick up. Shanghai firms initially thought that sales might be reduced due to the poor silkworm season in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, so they were afraid to stock up too much. However, seeing that sales were still brisk, they rushed to prepare. Unfortunately, the place of origin is far in the southwest of Hunan Province, and it was initially reported that transport was blocked along the way, so merchants were unwilling to sell in advance. Zhenjiang merchants also tightened their stocks as a result. Although it has recently been confirmed that the transport to western Hunan is not completely blocked, delays are inevitable. It is uncertain whether the goods on the way can meet the demand during the summer season, so it is certain that the supply will be scarce. Letters from Zhenjiang merchants have repeatedly detailed this, but Shanghai firms initially did not believe it. Later, they began to believe it when goods did not arrive. Fortunately, they currently have a decent amount of goods on hand, which should be enough to meet the needs of various places and prevent a shortage.

Metals: Tinplate Reaches Its Peak and Declines

The tinplate market was booming in the previous two months due to supply exceeding demand, and selling prices were soaring. However, recently, due to the flood of incoming goods and the impact of the rainy season, factories have suspended operations, and customers are unable to take in goods due to poor market conditions, so the market has gradually weakened and standards have strongly reverted. The current price for 90-pound British goods is estimated at only 14 taels and 5 qian, American goods at 16 taels, 100-pound British goods at 15 taels and 5 qian, American goods at 17 taels, and 200-pound Company Iron at 31 taels, a sharp drop of 1-5 taels compared to the previous market. However, trading remains sluggish, and market sentiment is secretly fatigued. The future market is difficult to be optimistic about.

Seven Hundred Bundles of New Lead Wire Newly Arrived

There has been no progress in the trading of new lead wire recently, mainly due to weak customer sales and abundant inventory. However, more than 700 bundles of new goods arrived at the New Taikoo Warehouse yesterday, further increasing the inventory and making the market more sluggish. However, due to the boycott of goods, it is impossible for Japanese goods to come to Shanghai. If sales to the northern customers and along the Yangtze River pick up, the market situation will be very optimistic. The current prices are 13 taels and 5 qian for sizes 16-20, and 18 taels and 7 qian and 5 fen for sizes 21-25.

Xiong Shihui's Victory Telegram

▲The Suppressing Bandit Army Occupied Ningdu City

Mayor Zhang received a telegram from Commander Xiong yesterday, saying, "Urgent, Chief of Staff Zhu of Nanjing, Mayor Zhang of Shanghai, Our Left Group Army occupied Ningdu City at 4 PM today, killing countless enemies. The remnants of the bandits fled west in defeat. Sincerely reported, Xiong Shihui Hao Hai Can Yin."

Shanghai Municipality Levies Business Tax

▲Regulations...Detailed Rules...Standards

▲Approved and Promulgated by the Central Government after Revision

The preparatory office for the Shanghai Municipal Business Tax has previously drafted business tax regulations, detailed rules, and tax rate tables, and invited representatives from chambers of commerce to hold meetings for discussion. After repeated research, the draft was submitted to the Finance Bureau, which then submitted it to the municipal government and forwarded it to the central government for approval. Recently, it was heard that the central government has revised the draft and sent it to the Shanghai Municipal Government for the Finance Bureau to announce. The revised drafts of the Shanghai Municipal Business Tax Regulations, Implementation Rules, and Taxation Standards are recorded in a separate special column.

The Central Urban Area Begins to Invite Land Acquisition

▲Registration Starts Today

The municipal government, in order to construct the central urban area, has designated more than 7,000 acres of land between Yinhang, Yinxiang, and Jiangwan. The intention is to prevent those with large amounts of capital from manipulating land prices, thereby hindering construction. Therefore, after purchasing the designated land, a portion will be divided and sold at a price of 2,000 yuan and 2,500 yuan, which only includes the cost of road construction and equipment. It will be offered to the public for citizens to build on. In recent days, major newspapers have carried large advertisements to publicize this, and it has been decided to start registering in sequence from today. No one may compete to be first, nor may they pre-register before today. It is said that those who go to register at that time will also be able to freely visit the site.

It is heard that in order to facilitate transportation in the area, the municipal government has decided that, in addition to constructing various main roads, the original Xiangyin Road, Songhu Road, Qimei Road, and other cinder roads will be converted into asphalt roads. In addition to Xiangyin Road, which has already started work, the other roads are also being prepared for construction by the Bureau of Public Works, which has hired workers and purchased materials. It is also understood that within the scope of this land acquisition, the Bureau of Public Works has dispatched personnel to measure and stake out road boundaries daily, so that road construction can begin immediately after the land acquisition.

Economic Severance with Japan and Movement to Resist Japanese Goods

▲ Telegram sent to all areas to investigate and confiscate Japanese goods

▲ Chamber of Commerce convenes a general membership meeting

Since the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee began its work, it has been extremely busy, especially with regard to the boycott of Japanese goods. The following is a record of various news items from yesterday:

▲ Telegram to Confiscate Goods: The committee yesterday sent a telegram to all provinces and cities, stating, "Party departments in all provinces and cities should forward this to all organizations. Shanghai has begun inspections. If Japanese goods are smuggled in, please detain them upon arrival at the port. Respectfully, Shanghai Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee."

▲ Inspections Begin: The committee's inspection department, noting that Japanese goods have recently been arriving and being transshipped in large quantities, has decided to begin inspections immediately.

▲ Registration Work: The inventory registration is now being handled by the registration section's director and deputy director, Chen Tingrui and Xi Yushu, who have drafted registration forms and are rushing to have them printed. Some people have already brought orders to register, but official registration is scheduled to begin on the afternoon of the 23rd.

▲ Standing Committee Meeting: The committee held its second standing committee meeting yesterday. Wang Yansong, Tao Baichuan, Hou Dachun, Lu Jingshi, Chen Tingrui, and others attended. Wang Yansong was publicly elected as temporary chairman. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Telegram all local party departments to forward to all organizations, stating that if Japanese goods arrive at the port, they should be detained. (2) Passed the staff service volunteer form and introduction guarantee. (3) Resolved that the general affairs section be divided into three sub-sections: documentation, general affairs, and accounting; the propaganda section be divided into two sub-sections: writing and lecturing; the inspection section be divided into two sub-sections: administration and intelligence, and a special inspection office be established; and the registration section be divided into three sub-sections: registration, compilation, and statistics. (4) Official registration procedures were decided to begin on the afternoon of the 23rd.

▲ Korean Expression: The committee received a telegram yesterday from the Korean National Association in the United States, stating, "To the Shanghai Korean Provisional Government, forwarded to the Chinese Anti-Japanese Association, the Korean people's anti-Chinese tragedy was a Japanese plot, not the intention of the Korean people. Please forgive us. Korean National Association in the United States."

▲ Chamber of Commerce General Meeting: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a report to the Civil Training Committee and the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating, "Regarding the matter of reporting: It has been found that the Japanese have increased armed police in Wanbaoshan, forcibly occupying farmland and engaging in provocative demonstrations. They have also incited ignorant Koreans to persecute overseas Chinese in various parts of Korea. These two cases have aroused public outrage throughout the country. Our city has organized an Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese General Assembly by all sectors of society, and has resolved to sever economic relations with Japan. The association held its 17th Executive Committee meeting yesterday and resolved to convene a temporary general membership meeting at 2:00 PM on the 24th of this month to discuss detailed methods for boycotting Japanese goods. This is being implemented. In addition to separate official reports, this document is hereby submitted for approval and record. Please send personnel to provide guidance at that time."

▲ Various Industries' Expressions: (1) The Ginseng and Bird's Nest Guild held an emergency temporary executive committee meeting yesterday, attended by all executive committee members. Chairman Zhu Binglu reported on the purpose of the meeting and proposed a discussion on voluntary methods for boycotting Japanese goods. It was resolved to appoint Chen Rangqing, Wang Zhujun, Ling Shoupeng, and Tong Baoqing as committee members to investigate Japanese goods, and to issue an emergency notice stating, "Regarding the matter of emergency notification: It has been found that the Japanese have instigated Koreans to massacre overseas Chinese compatriots. All of our countrymen are righteously indignant and express deep sympathy. An emergency meeting was convened on the 20th of this month, and it was unanimously resolved that all members of our industry shall not privately import Japanese goods from July 14th onwards. If Japanese goods have been purchased before the 14th, they should be returned immediately. All existing Japanese goods must be reported in detail to this association for registration within one week. In the future, if anyone privately imports Japanese goods again, once discovered, they will be punished most severely according to the methods to be discussed in the future. This is a sincere warning, and all must abide by it. Respectfully addressed to all precious firms, Shanghai Ginseng and Bird's Nest Industry Association." (2) The Shoe Industry Guild held its 18th Executive Committee meeting on the 16th and unanimously resolved to follow the methods of the Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee, to vigorously implement economic severance, boycott enemy goods, and notify fellow traders that they should not privately use Japanese goods before a satisfactory resolution is reached in the negotiations. It is hoped that all sectors of society will be of one mind and persist to the end.

Japanese Goods Amidst Anti-Japanese Sentiment

▲ Channels become smoother and transshipment becomes busier

▲ Cargo Ships Fully Loaded: More Japanese goods were transported to various ports along the Yangtze River yesterday. Export cargo ships from the six major companies were almost entirely loaded with Japanese goods. The Jianghua, Changxing, Lianhe, Changsha, Yueyang, and other ships of Sannorth, China Merchants, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Nisshin Steamship companies were all fully loaded yesterday, mainly with Japanese sugar and kelp.

▲ Cotton Goods Sell Out: Japanese cotton goods are selling very well. An investigation of the Dongyang cotton goods in the warehouses found a total of 16,300 pieces, which have been completely sold out from the 14th to yesterday.

▲ Additional Ships Transporting Goods: The Japanese trading company Kawasaki Kisen Kaisha in this port, due to the large amount of cargo and the shortage of ships, has telegraphed Japan to send the 2,500-ton Ryūhei Maru to Shanghai to join the North China route, specifically to load Japanese goods. In addition, the Nanhua route ship Zuishō Maru of the Daito Steamship Company has also been transferred to Shanghai in advance to help transport Japanese goods to Shantou, Xiamen, Guangdong, and other ports.

Korean Merchants' Transition After Incheon's Market Reopens

▲ Summer Cloth Merchants Begin Loading Goods Today

After the anti-Chinese riots by Koreans, trade between China and Korea completely stopped. The summer cloth industry alone suffered an intangible loss of 300,000 yuan. The Shanghai Korean Association received a telegram from the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Seoul, Korea, the other day, stating, "Minister Wang has arrived in Seoul and is consulting with local consuls and chambers of commerce to investigate the situation in detail. The market is now peaceful. Please do not worry." The Incheon Overseas Chinese telegraphed to the Shanghai Summer Cloth Guild, "The market has now reopened, but business is slow." However, seven companies in the summer cloth industry, including Hengshengdong, Deyu, Longhe, Tongheyong, Jusheng, Yuantai, and Liuyuji, because the peak season for summer cloth sales is June and July, with sales of Korean summer cloth reaching as many as 15,000 pieces in July last year, but due to the Korean incident, stocks in Shanghai are piled up like mountains. Now that Incheon has reopened its market, they are taking advantage of the Mitsubishi Company's Keian Maru, which will depart for Incheon at 12:00 AM today, to load 500 pieces of summer cloth bound for Incheon, all of which are summer cloth from Jiangxi and Sichuan.

Overseas Chinese Compatriots Return to Shanghai from Korea

Overseas Chinese compatriots Hu Fande, Hu Shaomei, Liu Cuiying, Hu Yuxian, and others who operated eyeglasses and watch shops on Nissen-machi in Gyeongseong, Korea, were attacked by Koreans and have already fled back to Shanghai on the Keian Maru, which arrived in Shanghai yesterday. In addition, Zhou Chenglie, Zhou Fenglin, Zhou Guanglian, Li Zhiyan, and others who worked in Busan, all from Qingtian County, Zhejiang, fled to the Busan Consulate during the Korean massacre of overseas Chinese. They were also sent by the consulate on the Keian Maru and arrived in Shanghai yesterday. Everyone escaped with their lives, but all their belongings were completely lost. Everyone who arrived in Shanghai was in a very disheveled state and has now returned to their ancestral homes in Qingtian.

Foreign Pilot Resumes Work Yesterday

▲ Pilotage Fee Issue to be Resolved by Arbitration Within Two Weeks

The 38 members of the Shanghai Foreign Merchant Pilot Association had been on strike for a week to demand revisions to the pilotage fee issue. It is now known that the Pilot Association has accepted the opinions of the pilotage authorities, and all pilotage fees were resumed at 11:00 AM yesterday. As for the issue of revising the pilotage fee, it will be submitted to arbitration and resolved within two weeks. This reporter visited the Harbour Master Green of the Customs Maritime Department and the Chairman of the Pilot Association, F.L. Philip, yesterday and both stated that pilotage work has now returned to normal.

▲ Customs' Letter of Notification: Green, acting Harbour Master of the Jianghai Customs, based on the decision of the pilotage authorities last Saturday, sent a letter to the Pilot Association stating, "Your letter of May 28 requesting revisions to the pilotage fee, etc., was discussed at a meeting of the pilotage authorities on July 13. At that time, the truth of this matter was not fully understood, and it was decided to postpone a decision pending a separate investigation by a special commissioner. The investigating commissioner will study the cost of living in this port and compare the pilotage fees charged by pilots in this port with those charged by pilots in other major commercial ports, and then submit his opinions to the pilotage authorities, stipulating a fair pilotage fee for Shanghai. As for how many ships each pilot should pilot each month, and how many pilots are normally required, these should also be noted in the report. I should then inform the pilotage authorities that the Inspector General of Customs is willing to have the customs accounting secretary conduct this investigation, and decide on the pilotage fee issue. The Consular Body and the Harmony Business Association have also approved this proposal. When your association held a meeting on July 14, the customs authorities notified you by telephone of this decision, stating that the investigation would take about a week, and hoping that work would be resumed during this investigation period. However, your association's letter of July 14 stated that it would not provide pilotage services for merchant ships until the conditions were accepted. This morning at 10:30 AM, the pilotage authorities held another meeting and decided that the pilots of your association should first resume work unconditionally, and wait for someone to conduct a thorough investigation of each person's situation before resolving the issue of revising the pilotage fee. Please notify the members of your association to resume work. As for the letters of introduction of each person, they will be returned. Please reply before 4:00 PM on July 20, otherwise the pilotage authorities will take measures."

▲ Pilots Resume Work: The Pilot Association immediately held a meeting yesterday morning to discuss and decided to accept the opinions of the pilotage authorities. A representative was then sent to the Harbour Master's Office of the Jianghai Customs to reply, and the letters of introduction were immediately retrieved at 11:00 AM, and all work was resumed. The Pilot Association then issued a statement resuming work. The pilotage strike thus came to an end.

Turkish Chargé d'Affaires Returned to His Country Yesterday

▲ Turkish Embassy Temporarily Suspends Operations

▲ Sino-Turkish Treaty to be Signed in Europe

Turkish Chargé d'Affaires Fu Tepei returned to his country by order of the Turkish government. Yang Nianzu, Director of the Foreign Affairs Office, was ordered by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to personally see him off at the wharf and presented him with a Hunan embroidery center screen gifted by Foreign Minister Wang. As for the Sino-Turkish treaty, the Turkish Chargé d'Affaires has already agreed with Foreign Minister Wang to sign it in Europe. The location will be in Paris or Geneva, and it will be jointly executed by our country's minister and the Turkish representative stationed there.

Airplane Lands in the Huangpu River

▲ Wusong Port Suddenly Encountered Wind and Rain

▲ Fuselage and Passengers Unharmed

The China National Aviation Corporation's airplane, flying from Beijing to Shanghai, encountered a sudden gale and rainstorm near Wusong Port yesterday afternoon, and landed in the middle of the Huangpu River there. It did not fly to Longhua Airport until several hours later, so the arrival time in Shanghai was slightly delayed. However, the airplane and passengers were unharmed.

According to the Daily News, two Japanese passengers, Suzuki and Imamura, drowned. This newspaper has conducted a detailed investigation and found that it is completely inaccurate.

Anhui Province is Overwhelmed with Calls for Help Due to Flooding

The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Relief Association previously received telegrams from Quanjiao, Bengbu, and the area along the Huai River, reporting that the floods had turned the area into a swamp. Now, urgent telegrams have also been received from Wuhe, Fuyang, Huaiyuan, Dingyuan, and other counties, all reporting floods and extremely dire situations, and needing urgent relief. Excerpts are as follows: (1) Wuhe is located in the lower reaches of the Huai River. This summer, incessant rain has raged, and the Huai River has risen more than ten feet. This month, there have been torrential rains all day long, and the dikes in all four directions have collapsed one after another. The water depth in the plains is as much as ten or twenty feet. Countless houses, people, and livestock have been washed away. At present, there is a lack of clothing, food, and shelter. Life hangs by a thread. We urgently hope for rapid relief to save those who are about to die. (2) Fuyang has suffered from drought and floods for years, with countless problems. Last autumn and this spring, the River God caused trouble. The disaster area is dozens of miles, and nine out of ten households are empty. Now, in June, there has been incessant rain for ten days, and the rivers have risen sharply. The vast water is boundless. Looking from the city, the whole area has turned into a swamp. Fields and crops have been washed away, and houses no longer exist. Among the hundreds of thousands of disaster victims, countless families have become subjects of waves and food for fish. Those who are fortunate enough to escape with their lives gather in swarms, looking emaciated and eating wild plants, exposed to dew and wind, with nowhere to settle. We respectfully beg for merciful broth and righteous grain to generously relieve the disaster victims. With disheveled hair and tied crowns, we anxiously await your aid day and night. (3) Huaiyuan is located in a low-lying area, like the bottom of a pot. This summer, there has been heavy rain for days, and mountain floods have erupted. The inside and outside of the city have all turned into a swamp. Hundreds of miles of villages, houses, fields, crops, and livestock have been washed away by the flood. Countless people have drowned. This is truly an unprecedented disaster. We mourn for the countless survivors. If we do not provide urgent relief, how can they survive? We respectfully implore you on behalf of 400,000 disaster victims. (4) In the western countryside of Dingyuan, mountain floods have erupted, and the Pei and Luo Rivers have flooded and caused disasters. Fields, houses, gardens, grain, silver, and money have all been swept away by the flood. The deaths of people and the washing away of graves and corpses have made the disaster the most severe ever seen. The cries of mourning are everywhere, and it is unbearable to hear. At present, countless houses have collapsed, and the whole town is in danger of destruction. Although it has not come to cannibalism, food is scarce. The situation is sad and difficult to describe, and starvation awaits urgent relief. It is said that the association has not only received reports from various counties in northern Anhui, but also from areas along the Yangtze River, such as Jiujiang and Jiangxi, which are also said to be suffering from waterlogging. Moreover, Guangdong is said to be experiencing major floods, and almost every province is suffering from disasters. Letters and telegrams are pouring in like snowflakes. It is truly difficult for a clever woman to cook without rice. They are extremely anxious and plan to seek assistance from all sectors.

Guangdong Overseas Chinese Business Association Raises Relief Funds for Guangdong Floods

The Guangdong Overseas Chinese Business Association in this city, because of the severe flooding in Guangdong, with more than a hundred embankment breaches and disaster victims everywhere, making the disaster even more severe than in the year of Yimao (1915), held a general membership meeting at the association at 2:00 PM yesterday to discuss urgent relief methods. More than 400 people attended the meeting, and Chen Bingqian was publicly elected chairman. He announced the reasons for the meeting. Everyone believed that the disaster situation in Guangdong Province was serious and that urgent relief should be raised. It was resolved that the association would immediately advance 10,000 yuan in Guangdong silver dollars and hand them over to the Guangzhou Convenient Hospital for distribution. The association will also launch a fundraising campaign, and the funds raised will be remitted to Guangdong in succession. Chen Bingqian, Xu Zouyun, Yang Runzhi, Guo Biao, Huang Huannan, Liu Xiji, Hai Chushan, Li Shuyu, Cui Pingxi, Deng Jieqing, Gan Rongchu, Ou Jingtang, Liang Haichou, Cheng Binghui, Lu Xisan, Li Rixi, Zhong Anqiao, Li Huasheng, Ma Lixing, Chuan Xiulun, Tang Yaojian, Yang Yichu, Yang Youzhi, Chen Yizhou, Feng Zuo, Liang Qingci, Chen Liting, Feng Chinan, He Quansheng, Zhang Zhuanchu, Fang Yusheng, and others were elected as members of the fundraising committee, and they set off to raise funds to save the survivors. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Early Departure Time for Beijing-Liaoning Train

▲ No Stops at Small Stations Along the Way

The Traffic Department of the Jinpu Railway Bureau had previously planned to change the departure time of the Beijing-Ping-Liaoning train to connect with the Beijing-Zhabei train of the Jinghu-Hangyong Railway. It is now known that starting yesterday (the 20th), the 201st train from Ping-Liaoning to Pukou will be made to depart earlier to connect with the 2nd Beijing-Zhabei train on the Jinghu Line. At the same time, it was announced that the 201st and 202nd trains on the Beijing-Ping-Liaoning route would no longer stop at small stations such as Dongge, Guandian, Hanzhuang, Wucun, Wande, Yancheng, Pingyuan, Xingji, Qingxian, etc., to shorten the time. As for the departure time, it remains the same.

Implementation of Direct Delivery of Postal Items Between China and Czechoslovakia

The Directorate General of Posts, in order to facilitate postal administration and simplify procedures for parcels sent from various ports in China to Czechoslovakia, which were previously forwarded to various parts of the country through Germany, recently established a postal service between China and Czechoslovakia with the Czechoslovakian postal authorities to handle the exchange of insured box containers. This method will be carried out by the two countries in accordance with the treaty from today. In the future, all goods imported and exported from various ports in China to Czechoslovakia will designate Shanghai and Guangzhou as the general areas for collection of items, and then the Shanghai and Guangzhou postal authorities will hand them over to French mail ships for transportation, via the Suez Canal, and then directly to Czechoslovakia. It is rumored that the Directorate General of Posts will issue an order to the post offices to handle the matter in accordance with the treaty within a few days.

Shanghai Shipping Merchants Oppose Hold Tax

▲ Plan to Request the Ministry of Finance to Cancel

The Ministry of Finance ordered the Jianghai Customs to collect a tax of one copper coin per ton of cargo exported from each ship's hold, which has aroused the opposition of all Shanghai shipping merchants.虞洽卿,袁履登, and何墨林 were publicly elected to visit the Chief of Customs Robert氏 to discuss this tax.

Page 14

Discuss how this tax is contrary to the suppression of smuggling, and various ship bureaus are difficult to recognize. The tax authorities are related to orders of the Ministry, it is difficult to be responsible, and the shipping merchant should request the Ministry of Commerce. Yesterday, local Shanghai shipping merchants have drafted a statement opposing this tax, and its reasons are the following four items: (1) Although hold cargo, although the tax is not high, the procedure is very troublesome, which is enough to hinder the ship's schedule, to the customs authorities, due to the collection of this tax, and added employees, is also difficult to compensate, (2) If each ship has smuggled valuable goods, mostly loaded in the hold, those on the deck, not rough goods i.e. fresh fruit etc., do not comply with the purpose of curbing smuggling, (3) To avoid danger, shipowners have the right to throw cargo overboard in times of danger, (4) Each ship has paid tonnage tax, and the tonnage tax is the whole ship's waterline, then deck cargo should not be taxed again. If Customs thinks that cargo outside the main hold should pay a special tax, then can Customs subsidize shipping merchants in times of half-loaded or empty ships, etc. This statement can be sent to the Ministry of Finance today,

Request to Negotiate with Various Countries on Free Submarine Practice

▲ Transmitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for Review

The Shanghai Shipping Guild believes that submarines of various countries freely practicing in the navigation lanes of merchant ships are prone to danger. The Shanghai Shipping Guild submitted separate reports to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Transportation, requesting negotiations to stop this. The reports and instructions from the Ministry of Transportation are recorded as follows:

▲ Shipping Association Report: "Report for Foreign Submarines to Freely Practice in Merchant Ship Navigation Lanes, Arbitrarily Floating and Sinking, Hidden Crisis, Dangerous Situation Easy to Happen, Sincerely Requesting to Notify the Ambassadors of Various Countries Stationed in China, (Consult the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Notify the Ambassadors of Various Countries Stationed in China) Strictly Restricting, In Order to Stop the Danger and Secure Safety. Foreign Submarines often Freely Practice in Navigation Lanes that Must Be Passed by Merchant Ships in China, Arbitrarily Floating and Sinking, and Their Practice Methods often take Merchant Ships as the Target for Trials, so whenever a Merchant Ship Approaches, those that are Floating must Immediately Sink, and those that are Sinking must Immediately Float, Appearances are Unusually Abrupt, Revolving Often Violates Fixed Rules, Merchant Ships Cannot Know in Advance in Navigation Lanes, and there is no way to foresee the changes that may happen. Thinking of the Situation that Hidden Crisis Dangerous Situation is Easy to Happen, Shipowners Sailors Passengers Cargo Owners are All Like Thorns in the Back, Unable to Pass a Day, If there is no way to Stop this, How Can We Ensure Safe Navigation and Protect Human Life, Therefore, Preparing this Document to Request Your Ministry, Quickly (Transfer Consultation with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs) Notifying the Ambassadors of Various Countries Stationed in China, In the Future, If There are Submarines Training and Practicing in Our Country's Merchant Ship Navigation Lanes, One Month in Advance, the Ambassador of that Country must Send to Your Ministry a Detailed Consultation Including the Ocean Area Longitudinal and Latitudinal Lines Start and End Dates and Times and the Number of Practicing Submarines, Requesting Your Ministry to Transfer the Instructions to the Maritime and Navigation Administration Agencies, Announcing to All National Merchant Ships, so That Everyone is Aware, and Temporarily Detouring to Avoid, Otherwise If Our Country's Merchant Ships Collide with Submarines, No Matter What is Right or Wrong, the Other Party is Responsible for Damages and Our Country's Merchant Ships Losses Shall Be Borne by the Other Party Without Limit of Compensation, In Order to Stop the Danger and Secure Safety, Presenting this with Impatience, Sincerely Presenting to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Ministry of Transportation."

(Item 5) Cele Company previously requested proof that Eroanier was not a narcotic drug. The company has now submitted a certificate from the Central Hygiene Testing Institute. Should this be used as the basis for proof? It was resolved to send another letter to the Central Hygiene Testing Institute to verify the reply before issuing a certificate. (Item 6) Nurses from other ports are requesting registration or seals. Should they be processed as requested? It was resolved that because it is currently limited to the scope of Shanghai, handling of matters from other ports should be temporarily delayed. (Item 7) Standing Committee Member Li Shenzheng has resigned. It was resolved to retain him. (Item 8) Physicians Fei Kunian, Li Shanjun, Liang Xianglan, Hu Lansheng, Zheng Zhiting, Liu Su, Ye Boyang, and Zhong Juemin have requested to join the association. It was resolved to approve the review.

Results of Distribution Registration of Silk Factories' Public Bonds

The issuance of Jiang-Zhejiang silk industry public bonds is imminent. The distribution method has been registered by the silk factories listing and submitting to the special committee. Among these public bonds, 2 million yuan will be used to improve machinery. The original amount was 2,000 yuan per black board machine and 3,000 yuan per cocoon boiling machine. Recently, because the cocoon boiling machine is too expensive, it has been increased to 4,000 yuan. As of now, there are 103 registered factories in Shanghai, about 40 in Wuxi, and 26 in Zhejiang. It has been submitted to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry yesterday. It is expected that the public bonds will be issued after review.

Resolution of Labor Dispute at Jinhua Dyeing Factory

The Jinhua Dyeing Factory on Ladu Road laid off 21 workers, including Xu Qiaosheng, at the end of June due to business reasons. Negotiations with the Dyeing Industry Union were unsuccessful, leading to a labor dispute. In order to resolve the situation quickly, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau convened labor and management for mediation, but it was still not resolved. At 9 AM yesterday, the Labor-Management Mediation Committee convened a meeting. Representatives from the management, Li Shouzhang and Yan Chuanji, and representatives from the labor, Liu Jintai and Lu Muqin, as well as Chairman Zhu Guilin, attended. After a long discussion, both parties agreed and signed the following agreement: (1) Fifteen temporary workers from the Jinhua Factory, including Wang Rui, etc., are allowed to terminate their employment relationship with the management. (2) Four workers, Bu Liubao, Wang Jincheng, Xu Qiaosheng, and Xia Changshou, are allowed to resume work immediately, and their wages during the layoff period will be paid as usual. (3) Two workers, Chen Baolin and Wang Zhenqiu, are allowed to resume work, but their wages during the layoff period will not be paid. If they do not return to work by the end of this month, it will be considered a voluntary dismissal.

Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company's Second Annual Meeting

Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Co., Ltd. convened its second annual shareholders' meeting the day before last at the Gaolangqiao factory on Huade Road. 120 shareholders with a total of 10,487 shares attended, meeting the legal quorum. Shen Zhongyi was publicly elected as chairman. First, he gave an opening speech. Then, General Manager Zhang Rongchu reported on the business situation. Then, Pan Xulun, an accountant, reported on the account summary. After Supervisor Lin Xiuliang contributed his opinion, the election of supervisors began. As a result, Lin Xiuliang, Shen Chuchen, and Yuan Rongbiao received the most votes and were elected as supervisors for this session. Next, the chairman raised a proposal regarding the future business policy, which should be decided by the general meeting. It was resolved to adopt the first option: after the contract period of the outsourcing expires, the company will operate on its own. How to handle it appropriately should be the full responsibility of the board of directors. Next, shareholder Qiu Maoru raised an opinion, stating that the company's products sometimes have discrepancies in yardage and size, and that the company's reputation should be maintained. It was resolved that the board of directors would be responsible, and that from that day on, the yardage of each piece would be set at 36 inches. Other important matters were then discussed, and the meeting adjourned for refreshments until 5:30 PM.

Lawyer He Xiaoyuan Practices in Shanghai

He Xiaoyuan, courtesy name Dafeng, is from Minhou County, Fujian Province. He is a graduate of Tsinghua School in Beiping, a Master of Arts in Political Economy from Columbia University in the United States, and a Doctor of Law from the University of Chicago. He is proficient in law and skilled in advocacy, and is also fluent in English and Russian. After returning to China, he held important positions in the former Ministry of Communications and served as the director of the land department of the Chinese Eastern Railway. He has also provided assistance in many legal matters. The Soviet-Russian agreement was largely drafted by He. In the 15th year of the Republic, when the European and American judicial delegations came to China to inspect the judiciary, he was hired by the Dong Province authorities to serve concurrently in publicity work when they arrived in Harbin. He is particularly enthusiastic about the recovery of consular jurisdiction. Shanghai is a cosmopolitan area with close contact between Chinese and foreigners, so negotiations are bound to occur. The success or failure of these negotiations is truly the focus of attention both at home and abroad. Therefore, he resolutely came to Shanghai and set up a law firm at No. 20 Keneng Road to handle all Chinese and foreign litigation, in order to protect human rights and serve the party and the country.

News from Trade Associations

▲ Western Pigment Industry: The Western Pigment Industry Association held a general meeting of representatives the day before last. The ceremony was held as usual. Two Dysentery Medications with Proven Efficacy

The Watery Diarrhea Medicine and Dysentery Pills produced by the Lao Tongchang Felt Carpet Shop on Jixiang Street in the French Concession have been sold for more than 80 years. They have unique and remarkable effects and are widely praised. Watery diarrhea is generally caused by catching a cold or eating too much raw and cold food, leading to abdominal pain and diarrhea. Dysentery is often caused by damp heat stagnation or the love of melons and fruits. The symptoms are red and white pus, and the discharge is sluggish. These medications can be taken in new and old cases. Those who have purchased them have been cured.

Local News Two

The Detective Division Appeals Regarding Liang Chengyu

▲ Correcting Errors in the Original Trial Verdict

▲ The Trial and Debate Concluded Yesterday

Liang Chengyu, a Chinese detective of the No. 2 Squad of the General Investigation Department of the General Police Station, was implicated in a morphine robbery case at 439 Malalei, Chongqing Road, on April 28th of this year at 11 PM, involving valuables worth 50,000 silver dollars belonging to Li Liansheng. The Municipal Council prosecuted him in the Special District Court under Article 348 of the Criminal Code for robbery. After several interrogations by Judge Ge, Liang Chengyu was declared innocent on June 2nd. Li Liansheng was also prosecuted by the detective division for suspected kidnapping of Li Huiqing, and the investigation is currently being rescheduled. However, the detective division, dissatisfied with the acquittal of Liang Chengyu in the morphine robbery case, had Boliang Rubao Yi, an acting lawyer for the Municipal Council, list the reasons and file an appeal to the Jiangsu High Court Branch.

▲ Four Reasons for the Appeal. At 11 AM yesterday morning, Song Yuan, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division of the High Court Branch, along with Judges Du and Gao, convened a hearing. The defendant, Liang Chengyu, retained the services of lawyers Ye Fukang, Yuan Yang'an, and Peng Jie to represent him. The representative lawyer of the detective division, Rubao Yi, began by stating that during the initial trial, the detective division had prosecuted based on Article 348 of the Criminal Code for robbery. All evidence at the time had been presented to the fullest extent possible by the detective division, and the defendant had also presented counter-evidence to prove his activities that evening. As a result, the original trial acquitted the defendant, but after receiving the verdict, the detective division carefully examined it and found it to contain significant errors. Therefore, they requested the court to remedy these errors, which can be divided into the following four points: (1) The original verdict stated, "The defendant vehemently denied it." It is common for defendants to deny and quibble in an attempt to escape guilt. Therefore, unless they can present strong counter-evidence, their mere denial cannot be accepted. In this case, the statements of the plaintiff, Li Liansheng, and his mistress, Zhang A'si, are of utmost importance. Although questioned separately multiple times, their accounts of the robbery and the circumstances before and after were detailed and consistent. Moreover, the plaintiff was able to immediately identify the defendant as one of the robbers in a crowd at the detective division, clearly indicating that the matter was not fabricated. (2) The original verdict also stated that the testimonies of Li Liansheng and Zhang A'si differed in many aspects. For example, Li stated, "I remembered that it was Mr. Zhang who informed them because after the guns were taken, I saw him send them to the defendant's home, and my woman, Zhang A'si, followed them." Zhang stated, "A woman named Zhang said that the guns were taken from 756 Chengdu Road." Such important matters had such discrepancies. Upon investigation, although the testimonies of the two individuals differed slightly, they were essentially the same. The Chengdu Road address provided by Zhang was the defendant's home mentioned by Li. Perhaps the judge who drafted the verdict did not pay attention to the defendant's residence, which led to the perception of discrepancies. Furthermore, upon close examination of the records, the testimonies of the two individuals were mostly consistent. Although the wording may have differed slightly, it was not of great significance. However, the original trial overlooked the numerous similarities and focused on the occasional differences, and even stated that the differences were numerous when they were clearly the same. The principle of evidence law was violated during the process of gathering evidence, so the verdict was difficult to be accurate and fair. (3) The original verdict also stated that Zhang A'si initially mistakenly identified Hua Tan Shen Tianbao, No. 110, as the defendant when she first arrived at the detective division, and therefore concluded that the identification was unclear and not sufficient to be used as evidence. However, there were five or six Chinese detectives standing together in the detective division at the time, and they had all removed their badges. Therefore, Zhang A'si initially pointed to No. 110 but then realized her mistake and immediately corrected it. This is a common occurrence and naturally there is a possibility of correction. (4) The original verdict also stated that Li Liansheng's suspicion was not without reason. At the time, the defendant claimed that Li Liansheng was Fang Liansheng, also known as Xiao Liansheng, and was involved in the Li Huiqing kidnapping case. He had attempted to arrest him several times without success, which led to the suspicion of false accusation. Upon investigation, Li Liansheng did not report the case to the detective division at the time. The detective division discovered the case and conducted a thorough investigation. Li was later apprehended in the French Concession, and it was not that Li turned himself in to the detective division. The reason Li did not report the case to the detective division was that Li had concealed morphine and committed robbery, which were both illegal acts, and may have been related to the kidnapping case. He did not report it until he was arrested and could not deny it, so he revealed it. Eight nights later, his mistress was also arrested. Therefore, the original trial's view of the suspicion was inappropriate. In summary, the full text of the judgment is based on these four reasons, but the detective division believes they are inappropriate and that sufficient evidence had been presented at the time to prove that the defendant had committed a crime. Therefore, they filed an appeal.

▲ Liang Chengyu Continues to Deny. Judge Song then questioned the defendant, Liang Chengyu, and asked, "Li Liansheng accused you of robbing morphine. Did this happen?" Liang replied, "Li Liansheng is Fang Liansheng, also known as Xiao Liansheng, and is involved in the kidnapping case of Li Huiqing. I have twice accompanied Western Detective Hunter and Chinese Detective Chief Liu Shaokui to the Gansidong Road in the French Concession to arrest him without success. The first time was on February 13th or 14th, and the second time was about three weeks later, which can be investigated. I know nothing about the morphine robbery." Judge Song then asked his lawyer if he had investigated this point. The lawyer stated that the defendant did go to the French Concession with the Western detective to investigate on February 15th, but it was fruitless and only happened once. Judge Song then asked Liang, "Have you been to Li Liansheng's home on Chengdu Road?" Liang replied, "No." He asked, "Were you at the small inn behind the Far Eastern Hotel on the night of April 28th?" Liang replied, "No." He asked, "How was this matter discovered?" Liang replied, "At this time, I had already taken leave because I received a telegram from my hometown in Shandong that my father had passed away, so I asked the Western Detective Chief for leave until May 4th, when I was called to the detective division by the Western Detective Chief."

▲ Li Liansheng's Testimony. Then, according to Li Liansheng's testimony, he worked as a hardware broker, Zhang A'si was his mistress, and he also had an old mother and wife at home, now living in Pudong Yangjing, his hometown. On March 11th, a fellow apprentice named Xu Gengen said that he had morphine and wanted to temporarily store it at my place, asking me to take it together with him. So I went with Xu and Zhang and others. I was on the road, and they went into the alley. After a short while, they took out four boxes. At first, we went to a friend's place on Dagu Road, but because it was discovered, we went to He Xing Fang on Jianshui Road, then to the Racecourse, and finally moved to the upstairs guest hall at 349 Malalei, Chongqing Road. The house was temporarily rented for fifteen yuan a month. At eleven o'clock at night, I suddenly heard someone knocking on the front door, asking if Liansheng was home. Before I could answer, a group of people entered through the back door and went straight to my room. There were six people in total. The defendant, Liang Chengyu, pointed a gun at me and threatened, "Be polite. We are detectives from the detective division. Hand over the morphine, and we will give you 3,000 yuan." I agreed, and they first carried away one box of morphine. When they came back, they had a handbag and put the remaining three boxes into the handbag and carried them out. Because it was late at night, they were stopped by the concierge at the entrance of the alley, so they turned back and押me and my mistress to a small inn to monitor us. It was not until dawn that they押ed Zhang A'si and me back home and took away the remaining morphine. Zhang A'si also gave a statement, which was slightly the same as Li Liansheng's. Omitted.

▲ Dong Lantings Testimony. Also, according to the witness Dong Lanting, he was a friend of Liang Chengyu. On the evenings of April 27th, 28th, and 29th, from 7 PM to 9 PM, I met Liang in Sheng Ping Li in the French Concession. Because Liang's father had passed away, he received a telegram and wanted to return to his hometown, so he asked me to take care of his family. We parted before 12 o'clock, and I don't know anything else.

▲ A Fierce Debate. At this point, the testimonies of the witnesses were completed, and the debate began. The defendant's lawyers, Ye Fukang, Peng Jie, and Yuan Yang'an, and the detective division's lawyer, Rubao Yi, stood up one after another and debated vigorously. For a while, there was a war of words, each displaying their eloquence. The debate lasted for about an hour before it ended. Finally, Prosecutor Zheng stood up and expressed his opinion, stating that after examining the circumstances of the case, the facts were clear. The witness presented by the defendant's side could not prove with certainty what the defendant did on April 28th, and the telegram presented by the defendant was actually prepared in advance to use as an excuse when committing a crime. He requested that the court make a judgment according to the law. Judge Song reviewed the report and announced the end of the debate, scheduling the pronouncement of the verdict for the morning of the 27th. Liang Chengyu was detained and not allowed bail. By the time the hearing was over, it was already 2:30 PM.

▲ A Large Quantity of Books Discovered

Huang Kai Attempts Suicide in Huangpu River and is Rescued

▲ A Suicide Note and a Suicide Poem

Huang Kai, a native of Jiaxing, 22 years old, had received considerable education. He previously served as a quartermaster sergeant in the Independent First Battalion, Second Company, of the Special Tax Police Regiment of the Ministry of Finance. Now that the regiment has been abolished, he was sent back to his hometown. However, his relatives at home, seeing that he was extremely poor and bored, all looked at him with disdain. Huang, stimulated by this, had no face to stay at home, so he took a car to Minhang. Yesterday morning, he changed to the Pinghu ferry and came to Shanghai. At about 1 PM, when it arrived at the Nanguan Bridge pier in Nanshi, just as it was about to dock, Huang suddenly had a thought of ending his life, left two suicide notes and a basket of golden melons, and jumped into the Huangpu River to commit suicide. Fortunately, he was rescued by the ferryman, who bravely made an effort, and sent to the Customs Water Police Station. After inquiring about the situation, the Chinese detectives collected more than four silver dollars for him and ordered him to find another job to make a living. The suicide note is recorded below:

I am a young man who is oppressed by the environment and has no possibility of struggling. However, I have also received secondary education, and I have a considerable understanding of military affairs and politics. After some time of training, I never liked to be subservient or follow the trend, especially since I grew up in a poor family. The word "friend" is not worth mentioning at all. Thinking back to the time when I used my knowledge, I once met people in society, and I worked very hard, but the result was disappointment, pain, and the word "suicide." Suicide is originally a boring action, or it can be said to be the result of a weak will, but I actually think it is the only god. Now I will travel with the world. Attached is a poem of seven quatrains: Floating in the dust for twenty-two springs, Looking back on the past years, dreams are frequent, World affairs are floating clouds, nothing but illusion, May my life return to the true with the water gods.

Illicit Lovers Stab Husband to Death

▲ The Murderer was Apprehended the Same Night

▲ Wang Hongding Confesses Without Hesitation

Yan Anong, 32 years old, a native of Pingyang, Zhejiang, made a living by fishing. His wife, Ms. Wu, 29 years old, had an affair with her neighbor, Wang Hongding, before she was married. After she married Yan, she never met him again. In the spring of this year, Yan led his wife to Shenjiamen outside the Wusongkou to fish. Unexpectedly, Wang Hongding was also there, making a living by net weaving. Then Yan and his wife met. He often went to Yan's house and pretended to be friends with Yan, but secretly continued his old affair with Ms. Wu. Yan knew nothing about it. Later, Yan's fishing in Shenjiamen was not profitable, so he took his family and Wang to live in Shengshan. Wang introduced Yan to borrow 50 silver dollars from the fish market as fishing capital, and the account would be settled after the fish was caught. Unexpectedly, Yan's fate was not good, and fishing was still very unprofitable, and the borrowed capital was completely exhausted. Wang repeatedly urged Yan to pay back the money, and Yan became angry and beat Wang violently. Wang had an affair with Ms. Wu and regarded Yan as a thorn in his side. After being beaten, he was very resentful, so at about 1 AM the day before yesterday, he sneaked into Yan's bedroom and stabbed Yan's abdomen with a sharp knife while Yan was sound asleep, breaking a hole and causing his intestines to bleed. Yan cried out loudly and died immediately. After Wang succeeded, he fled immediately. Ms. Wu heard the sound and came out to see her husband lying dead in a pool of blood, which was unbearable to see. Knowing that Wang had done it, she immediately reported to the 16th Team of the 4th District of the Water Police. Fortunately, the murderer Wang Hongding had not escaped far and was captured by the water police that night. He was escorted to the 4th District of the Wusong Water Police Department yesterday morning. After being interrogated by Section Chief Gong Pengzhu, who was assigned by District Chief Jiang, the murderer Wang Hongding confessed that he had an affair with Ms. Wu and that he resented being beaten for debt collection and committed the murder. Section Chief Gong reviewed the confession and ordered that he be escorted to the Chongming County Government for handling.

Recent Events of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps

▲ The Efficient Shield Western Team Wins

▲ The Chinese Team Ranks Second

▲ The Chinese Team is the Runner-up in the Japan Cup

The Efficient Silver Shield, a competition among the teams of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps, is the most difficult award to win in the entire corps. The Chinese team ranked second, and the Western team ranked first. At the same time, the Western team also won the Japan Cup with a score of 246.12, which was higher than the Chinese team's score of 241.97. The course of the cup competition is extremely complicated, and it is more difficult than the above-mentioned Efficient Silver Shield. Therefore, it is not easy for the Chinese team to win the runner-up in the past two years. The tree is a century-old cycad that suddenly bloomed this year and can treat women's heart pain and other diseases. The leaves of the cycad have completely fallen off, leaving only yellow flowers in the middle, the larger ones are about a foot long, and the smaller ones are three or four inches long, with a surrounding diameter of about three inches.
