Yihe Wharf Busts Smuggling Opium Case

▲ Six Sacks Worth More Than 4,000 Yuan

▲ Wang Guisheng and Others Detained for a Year and a Half

Liu Yongxiang, a Chinese detective from the Hongkou Detective Division, received a report from an informant that a large amount of opium was coming from the Longhe Steamer from Hankou at the Yihe Wharf on Yuanfang Road. He reported to the head detective and cooperated with detectives such as Zhang Yuting to disguise themselves as coolies at the wharf, each wearing weapons. At 3:15 AM yesterday morning, they secretly waited and watched. After a while, Wang Guisheng from Wuxi, Zhang Baozhen from Tianjin, and Jin Xiaoxizi from Qingkou arrived one after another and hired sampan boats to take six sacks of opium from the ship ashore. Just as they were about to load it somewhere, Detective Liu and others rushed forward and arrested Wang Guisheng and the other three, and took the opium together back to the detective division for detention. At about 8 o'clock, they were escorted to the Third Court of the Special Court. Li Zhishan, the detective division's lawyer, stated the case and said that the opium weighed 2,604 taels and was worth more than 8,000 yuan. The detective division is now accusing the three defendants of selling opium under Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law and asking for a strict investigation. Then, Detective Liu reported the circumstances of the incident and presented the opium for inspection. Wang Guisheng confessed that he did not know the source of the opium and that a friend named Xiaoliuzi came to him at the time and asked him to help transport it, promising to give him several silver dollars. He did not know where to send it or who the principal was. The others gave vague answers, and Zhang Baozhen and Jin Xiaoxizi confessed the same thing and asked for leniency. Judge Xiao Xiexun reviewed the confession and sentenced the three defendants, Wang Guisheng and others, to one year and six months of imprisonment each, and each was fined 2,000 yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, the fine shall be converted into imprisonment based on the ratio of the total amount of the fine to the number of days in a year. The number of days of detention before the final judgment shall be offset against one day of imprisonment for every two days. The opium was confiscated.

Fisherman Loses Arm

Around 7:00 PM last night, at the intersection of the west branch of South Station Road on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, a military train arriving at the South Station from Beijing was decoupling its locomotive, engine number 15. While passing along the tracks on the west branch, a man, appearing to be a fisherman around fifty years old, carrying a fishing net on his shoulder, attempted to cross the tracks. The locomotive arrived too quickly, and he couldn't avoid it, resulting in him being struck and having his left arm severed. He was bleeding profusely and unable to speak. The stationmaster dispatched police to rescue him, but his left arm was already severed. Subsequently, a railway police officer, Gu Hongye, along with station workers, carried him to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. It is reported that the injured fisherman is named Zhou Yushan, a 56-year-old local resident.

Murdered Man Found in Huangpu River

▲ Suspected Murder and Body Abandoned in the Huangpu River

At 9:00 AM yesterday, an unidentified male corpse was found floating on the Huangpu River surface near the Guangdong Road pier. It was retrieved by Chinese Constable No. 65 of the Customs Water Police Station and brought to the station. The corpse appeared to be about thirty years old, dressed in a blue long gown of "Liberty Cloth," a white vest with blue willow stripes, a white undershirt, and white twill trousers. He had a leather belt around his waist, a flat-top haircut, white Western socks, and black leather shoes. Both feet were bound with rope, indicating a clear case of murder. There were no belongings found near the body, presumably because the perpetrator feared leaving any traces that could lead to their capture. It is assumed that the murder was carefully planned over a long period of consideration before being carried out. The corpse is currently being held at the coroner's office by order of the police chief, transported there by the Life-Saving Bureau's patrol boat. Detective Wu Wenqing has been assigned to report to the local court this morning to have personnel examine the body for injuries, pending further investigation.

Special Item

Shanghai Municipality Business Tax Regulations (Revised)

Article 1. These regulations are formulated based on the central government's promulgated Business Tax Law. Article 2. Within the municipal area, all businesses, excluding factories subject to the central government's excise tax or companies and banks subject to special taxes, shall pay business tax in accordance with these regulations. Article 3. Businesses that meet any of the following conditions shall be exempt from business tax after verification: (1) Those taxed based on capital, with operating capital of less than 500 yuan. (2) Those taxed based on operating income, with an annual operating income of less than 1,000 yuan. (3) Businesses operated by the state or the municipality. (4) Non-profit businesses. (5) Businesses designated as exempt from business tax by central laws and regulations. Article 4. The tax base and tax rate for business tax are specified separately in a schedule. Article 5. For the sale of goods, if it is a wholesale business, the business tax on the wholesale portion may be paid at one-quarter of the fixed rate. The wholesale business mentioned in the preceding paragraph refers specifically to wholesale to other businesses in the same industry. If retail sales are also conducted in addition to wholesale, the tax amount shall still be calculated separately. Article 6. The calculation of operating capital shall be based on the paid-up capital. However, various reserve funds of limited companies shall be regarded as capital and taxed at one-third of the capital amount. Article 7. If various businesses have branches or factories within the city, their business tax may be paid jointly by the head office or head factory. If the head office, head factory, or branch has been established outside the city, the business tax shall be paid exclusively by the branch or factory or head office or head factory located within the city. If the capital cannot be divided and calculated, the tax collection agency shall estimate the taxable amount. If there is disagreement, it shall be handled in accordance with Article 13. Article 8. For businesses with multiple types of operations and different tax rates, the calculation of tax amount shall be based on the business and determined according to the main part of its operation. Article 9. Manufacturers who directly retail their manufactured products at their manufacturing location shall still be taxed at the tax rate stipulated for manufacturing. The directly retailed portion shall not be subject to business tax for retail businesses separately. Article 10. For businesses with the amount of operating income or capital and other calculated amounts as the tax base, the tax collection agency shall determine the total annual tax amount based on the estimated amount of annual operating income or the capital amount and the amount calculated by other methods, according to the tax rate, and apportion it to the four seasons for collection once each season (the amount collected each season is one-quarter of the annual tax amount). For newly established businesses, the business tax shall be calculated from the season of commencement. Article 11. When business tax is first implemented, for all types of industrial and commercial businesses, the tax collection agency shall send personnel to cooperate with the chamber of commerce to conduct investigations in accordance with the following provisions and prepare a tax collection list. The business tax investigation certificate shall be filled out, stamped by the respective industry association, and requested by the chamber of commerce to be transferred to the tax collection agency for issuance. If there is no industry association, the chamber of commerce shall request the transfer on their behalf. Subsequently, in the first month of the following year, the business operator shall fill out and submit a report requesting renewal of the business tax investigation certificate. The procedure shall be the same. For newly established businesses, the report shall be submitted before commencement. (1) The type and name of the business and its location. (2) The name, place of origin, and address of the business operator. (3) The amount of operating capital. (4) The estimated amount of annual operating income. The business tax investigation certificate mentioned in the preceding paragraph shall be renewed annually without any certificate fee. Article 12.

Page 16

For businesses with the amount of operating income and the amount calculated by other methods as the tax base, the business operator shall settle the amount of operating income or the amount calculated by other methods once at the end of each year and report it to the tax collection agency before January 15 of the following year. However, if the business terminates in less than one year, it shall be reported at the time of termination. Article 13. If the business operator fails to report in accordance with Articles 11 and 12 or makes a false report, the tax collection agency may send personnel to investigate and verify the taxable amount. If there is disagreement, the tax collection agency shall submit it to the Finance Bureau for referral to the review committee for assessment. The same shall apply to disagreement with the decision of the tax collection agency when business tax is first implemented. The investigation mentioned in the preceding paragraph shall be conducted by the tax collection agency in conjunction with representatives of the chamber of commerce and the industry association. Article 14. The organization and review rules of the review committee shall be determined separately. Article 15. When collecting business tax, the tax collection agency may, when necessary, inspect the business operator's books, documents, goods, and other items, but it must be done in conjunction with the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. Without the resolution and permission of the review committee, the business operator's books, documents, goods, and other items shall not be taken out of the inspected store or factory for investigation and inspection. Article 16. If a business operator suspends operations, transfers ownership, relocates, reorganizes, or increases capital, they shall immediately report it to the tax collection agency and separately surrender the old certificate and obtain a new certificate. Article 17. If a business tax investigation certificate is lost or damaged, a new certificate shall be obtained, and a fine of two dimes shall be paid. Article 18. If a business operator reports a larger or smaller amount of operating income or capital and other calculated amounts than the actual amount, conceals information, operates without a certificate, or delays tax payment, once discovered or reported, the tax collection agency shall submit it to the Finance Bureau for referral to the review committee for review and punishment. The penalties shall be determined separately. Article 19. The Finance Bureau shall notify the collection of business tax and fines once a month and prepare a credit record annually, which shall be reviewed, signed, and announced by the review committee. Article 20. Various donations and taxes in this city that are similar in nature to business tax shall be temporarily converted to business tax at the original tax rates. Article 21. For businesses not listed in the schedule of Article 4 of these regulations but that are subject to business tax, the Finance Bureau may propose the tax rate to be levied and submit it to the municipal government for consultation with the Ministry of Finance for review and approval before implementation. Article 22. The implementing rules of these regulations shall be determined separately. Article 23. These regulations shall be implemented after the municipal government consults with the Ministry of Finance for review and approval and announces them.

Shanghai Municipality Business Tax Regulations Implementing Rules (Revised)

Article 1. These implementing rules are formulated in accordance with Article 22 of the Shanghai Municipality Business Tax Regulations. Article 2. The Finance Bureau shall establish offices to handle the collection of business tax, taking into account local conditions. However, in special circumstances, it may entrust other agencies to handle it. Article 3. All businesses within the municipal area that meet the conditions for business tax shall comply with the provisions of Article 11 of the Shanghai Municipality Business Tax Regulations and apply for a business tax investigation certificate. Article 4. Business operators shall keep books and records, recording the following items: (1) Detailed number of goods and raw materials purchased. (2) Detailed number of goods sold. (3) Daily detailed records of cash receipts and payments. (4) Monthly totals. (5) Annual totals. Article 5. The tax collection agency shall prepare a business tax list, classifying and recording the items specified in Article 11 of the Shanghai Municipality Business Tax Regulations. The format of the list shall be determined separately. Article 6. The amount of business tax payable by a business operator shall be reviewed and determined by the tax collection agency upon the investigator's investigation report or the business operator's report. Article 7. Once the tax collection agency has determined the amount of business tax payable by a business operator, it shall not be reduced or increased within one year, unless otherwise provided by laws and regulations. Article 8. If a business meets the tax requirements, its annual operating income or capital amount and other amounts calculated by other methods are less than 1,000 yuan, the tax shall be calculated by rounding to the nearest whole number. Article 9. When collecting business tax, the tax collection agency shall fill out the receipt voucher quarterly and hand it over to the collection officer to collect with the voucher. Article 10. The business tax investigation certificate of a business operator shall be displayed in a conspicuous place for inspection. The business tax investigation certificate mentioned in the preceding paragraph shall be manufactured and issued by the Finance Bureau. Article 11. The report form and the fine receipt to be filled out by the business operator when applying for a business investigation certificate shall be manufactured and issued by the Finance Bureau for use by the tax collection agency. The format shall be determined separately. Article 12. If a business operator disagrees with the amount of tax assessed when paying business tax, the tax collection agency shall describe the investigation situation in detail, and if there is evidence, submit the evidence to the Finance Bureau for handling in accordance with Article 13 of the Shanghai Municipality Business Tax Regulations. Article 13. If the business operator's report on the taxable standard amount is certified by the chamber of commerce or a certified public accountant (limited companies shall be certified by a certified public accountant), the investigation procedure may be waived, but if the tax collection agency has doubts, it shall still be handled in accordance with Article 13 of the Shanghai Municipality Business Tax Regulations. Article 14. Businesses jointly operated by government and merchants shall still be subject to business tax. Article 15. If there are any matters not covered in these implementing rules, the Finance Bureau may revise them at any time and report them to the municipal government for approval and record. Article 16. These implementing rules shall be implemented after the municipal government consults with the Ministry of Finance for review and approval and announces them.

Shanghai Market

Market News

▲Universal Specialized Printing Company announces that the original business department is no longer sufficient for its needs, and has now moved to a five-story building at 141 Tiantong Road, North Bank of the Erbai Du Bridge, and will continue to operate as usual. If you are kind enough to patronize us, please move to the new address for consultation. Telephone number 41324.

▲City Inner Old North Gate Competition Company announces that our company has newly created a hunting game, a noble toy for children, with extraordinary fun and low price. Each set sells for only eight dimes (yuan). Major stores and bookstores in this city and other places are selling it.

▲Xiangtai Woodware Shop, across from Gezhi Public School on Guangxi Road, announces that our shop has always been known for genuine goods and fair prices. Recently, we have specially hired technicians to create art wood beds, which are exquisite, beautiful, and reasonably priced. Therefore, sales are quite broad.

▲Pathe Company on Renji Road announces that the films produced by our company in recent years have improved exceptionally. The recently invented four-and-a-half-minute records have achieved excellent results and are unrivaled in Shanghai. However, they have been promoted for a long time but have not yet been released. This is because we want to be cautious. The first batch will be officially released in the shortest possible time, including Mei Lanfang's "Farewell My Concubine", "The Legend of Taizhen", "Ding Shan Hunts Geese", and "Yang Guifei", Ma Lianliang's "Nanyang Pass", "Black Basin Case", "Four Scholars", "Hongyang Cave", "Imperial Stele Pavilion", "Stealing the Lineage Scroll", "Iron Lotus", and the Mei and Ma duet "Fisherman's Revenge" and "Four Lang Visits His Mother" and "Baolian Lantern" and many other pieces.

▲Maochang Optical Company, west of the old North Gate on Minguo Road, announces that recently, due to the hot weather and terrible sunlight, in order to protect the eyesight of people from all walks of life, we are selling various sunglasses. Once worn, even under sunlight, you will feel exceptionally clear and comfortable. They are essential items for summer. The price is low, and it is said that each pair sells for only one yuan.

▲Tongchang on North Shishi Road announces that our company's purpose is to promote Xia Bu (summer cloth) from various provinces. Since we held a 10% discount sale a few days ago, the sales of various goods have been very smooth, especially wholesale to other places. Although our company's selling price is lower, it is also really a result of the people's love of wearing domestic products. There are only six days left in the price reduction period, ending on the 25th. It is expected that there will be an even greater boom in these few days.
